[බාධා කිරීමක්] ඔච්චර ශබ්ද කරනවා. ඔබතුමා ඒ ෙගොල්ලන්ෙග් පිහිෙටන් අද ඡන්ද කරන්ෙන්. ඒ ෙගොල්ලන් පාවිච්චි කෙළේ ඡන්දය කාලෙය්. ඡන්දයක් ඉවර වුණු හැටිෙය්ම ආෙයත් ඇතුළට දමනවා. ඒ කාලෙය් ඔන්න, පෙද්ශයක් අල්ලනවා. අරක කරනවා. ෙම්ක කරනවා. දැන් ෙමොනවාද ෙවලා තිෙබන්ෙන්? දැන් ආපසු සබරගමුව ඡන්දය ළං වන විට යුද්ධයක් කරාවි. ඊට පස්ෙසේ කියාවි, අලි ෙකොටි ගිවිසුමක් ගැන. ඡන්දය නැති කාලෙය් කියයි, අලියා දැන් ජනතා විමුක්ති

[ගරු රවි කරුණානායක මහතා]

2008 ජුනි 19 629 630

ෙපරමුණත් එක්ක ඉන්නවාය කියා. ඊට පස්ෙසේ කියයි, රවුෆ් හකීම්ලාත් එක්ක ඉන්නවාය කියා. ඒ ෙගොල්ෙලෝ එක්ක විතරයි නැත්ෙත්. ඇයි, 2006 දී අෙප් එක්සත් ජාතික පක්ෂෙයන් සහෙයෝගය ඉල්ලන්න ෙමොකටද ආෙව්? එෙහම නම් ෙමොකටද ආෙව් අලියාට උදවු කරන්න? ෙමොනවාද ෙම් කරන්න හදන්ෙන්? රාජɕ ෙසේවා ෙකොමිෂන් සභාව තිබුණා නම් ෙම් අහිංසක රජෙය් ෙසේවකයන්ට සියයට 25කින් පඩි වැඩි කරනවා, සමස්තයක් වශෙයන්. අඩු ගණෙන් රුපියල් 7500ක් වැඩි කරන්න ඕනෑය කියන එක මම නැවත මතක් කරනවා. ගුරුවරුන්ට අද පශ්න තිෙබනවා. අහිංසක සිසුන් මහන්සි ෙවලා පාඩම් කරලා විභාගයට ඉදිරිපත් ෙවනවා. ඊට පස්ෙසේ ඒ ෙගොල්ලන්ෙග් විභාග පතිඵල ලබා ගන්නට හැකියාවක් නැහැ. ෙමොකද, ඒ අය ගිහිල්ලා answer scripts ටික බලන්ෙන් නැහැ. ෙම්වා සම්බන්ධෙයන් තමයි අපි කියන්ෙන් රාජɕ ෙසේවා ෙකොමිෂන් සභාවක් තියන්න කියලා. ෙම්කට ෙද්ශපාලන අරමුණක් අවශɕ නැහැ, මහින්දානන්ද අලුත්ගමෙග් ඇමතිතුමනි. ඇමතිතුමා ෙමතැන කෑ ගැහුවට, ජයතිස්ස රණවීර ඇමතිතුමා කෑ ගැහුවට - ගරු ජයතිස්ස රණවීර මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ஜயதிஸ்ஸ ரணᾪர) (The Hon. Jayatissa Ranaweera) නැහැ, මම කෑ ගහන්ෙන් නැහැ. ගරු රවි කරුණානායක මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ரவி கᾞணாநாயக்க) (The Hon. Ravi Karunanayake) ඇත්ත වශෙයන්ම හෘදය සාක්ෂිය අතගා බැලුෙවොත් "ඔව්, අර රවිලා කියන එක හරියි" කියයි. [බාධා කිරීම්] ඕනෑ තැනක් උරගා බලන එක ඔය ෙගොල්ෙලෝ කර ගන්න. ෙම් තුළින් අපි කියන්ෙන් කරුණාකර ෙම් රෙට් රජෙය් ෙසේවෙය් ස්වාධීනත්වය ඇති කරන්න කියලායි. ඒෙකන් තමයි ෙම් පශ්නය විසඳන්න පුළුවන් වන්ෙන්.

ෙදොස්තරවරුන් ගැන බලන්න. සියයට 25කින් ඇයි, ඒ ෙගොල්ලන්ට පඩි වැඩි කරන්න බැරි? [බාධා කිරීම්] අපි නිර්ධන පන්තිය නිෙයෝජනය කරනවාය කියලා, අපි ටයි, ෙකෝට් දමනවා කියනවා. ඇයි, සරම ඇඳලා තමුන්නාන්ෙසේලාෙග් ෙවෙළඳ ඇමති ෙමොනවාද කර තිෙබන්ෙන්? මම ෙකෝට් එක ඇඳලා රුපියල් 12ට දුන්න පාන් රාත්තල දැන් රුපියල් 50ට විකුණනවා. දැන් ෙමොනවාද කියන්ෙන්? මම රුපියල් 19ට දුන්න පිටි කිෙලෝ එක දැන් රුපියල් 70ට ගිහින් තිෙබනවා. [බාධා කිරීම්] ෙරද්ද, බැනියම ඇඳපු එක් ෙකනා ෙමොනවාද කරන්ෙන්, දකුණින් ආව අය ෙමොනවාද කරන්ෙන් කියා මම අහනවා. ෙමොනවාද ෙම් කරන විහිළු? අඳින එක ගැන කථා කරනවා. උස එක් ෙකෙනක් ගැන කථා කරනවා. විළි ලජ්ජාවක් නැද්ද? යුද්ධය පැරදුෙණොත් ජනමාධɕයට ගහනවා. ඒ අයෙග් ආයතනත් ගන්න හදනවා. ඉතින්, ෙමොනවාද? ඔබතුමාලා දන්ෙන් නැහැ කියා අපි ෙනොදන්නවායැ? Judgesලාටත් අය වැය ෙවනකම් ඉන්න කියා තිෙබනවා. කරුණාකර, යුද්ධ හමුදාෙව් අයට, ෙපොලීසිෙය් අයට, ගුරුවරුන්ට, ෙදොස්තරවරුන්ට වහාම රුපියල් 7500ක ෙහෝ සියයට 25ක ෙහෝ පඩි වැඩි වීමක් ලබා ෙදන්න. රාජɕ ෙසේවා ෙකොමිෂන් සභාව තිබුණා නම් අනිවාර්යෙයන් ෙම්ක ලබා ෙදනවා. අද උද්ධමනය කීයද? උද්ධමනය සියයට 33යි. අද Finance Commission එකක් නැති නිසා තිෙබන පශ්නයක් ෙම්ක. දැන් Finance Commission එකක් තිබුණා නම්, අනිවාර්යෙයන්ම මහ බැංකුව කරන විහිළුව කරන්න ඉඩ ෙදන්ෙන් නැහැ. ගරු මහින්දානන්ද අලුත්ගමෙග් මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு மஹிந்தானந்த அᾦத்கமேக) (The Hon. Mahindananda Aluthgamage) Finance ෙකොමිසම ෙනොෙවයි, මුදල් ෙකොමිසම.

ගරු රවි කරුණානායක මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ரவி கᾞணாநாயக்க) (The Hon. Ravi Karunanayake) ඕනෑ ෙකොමිසමක්. අහෙගන ඉන්න ෙකෝ. මට ඕනෑ භාෂාෙවන් මම කථා කරන්නම්. මෙග් දුර්වලතා තිෙබන්න පුළුවන්. මෙග් ආකාරයට මම වචන පාවිච්චි කරනවා. ඔබතුමාලා කථා කරන විධියට කථා කරන්න ඕනෑයැ? හරය ෙනොදන්නා ෙම් අය නිකම් jack-in-the-box වාෙග් කෑ ගහනවා. නාවලපිටිෙය් පාෙද්ශීය සභාවට ගිහින් ඔය ශබ්ද කරන්න. ගරු මන්තීවරෙයක් (மாண்ᾗமிகு உᾠப்பினர் ஒᾞவர்) (An Hon. Member) ඇයි සැර? ගරු රවි කරුණානායක මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ரவி கᾞணாநாயக்க) (The Hon. Ravi Karunanayake) ඇයි, සැර කියා අහන්ෙන්? අපිට කැක්කුමක් තිෙබනවා. ෙමතැන නාස්ති වන හැම මිනිත්තුවකටම ෙකොළඹ දිස්තික්කෙය් මෙග් අහිංසක ජනතාව ෙගවනවා. එෙහම ෙගවන ෙකොට සියයට 33ක උද්ධමනයටත් ෙගවනවා. ෙම් රෙට් සිදු වන දූෂණයටත් ෙගවනවා. ෙම් ආණ්ඩුව පුළුවන් තරම් ඉක්මනට එළියට යවන එක තමයි අවශɕ වන්ෙන්. [බාධා කිරීමක්] ගරු ජයතිස්ස රණවීර මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ஜயதிஸ்ஸ ரணᾪர) (The Hon. Jayatissa Ranaweera) ෙමොනවා කිව්වත් ඡන්දෙයන් අපි දිනනවා. ගරු රවි කරුණානායක මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ரவி கᾞணாநாயக்க) (The Hon. Ravi Karunanayake) ඔය ෙගොල්ලන් ඡන්දෙයන් දිනන්ෙන් නැහැ ෙන්. ඔබතුමාලා ගහලා ෙහොරකම් කළාම ඡන්දයක් තියනවායැ? ගරු ජයතිස්ස රණවීර මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ஜயதிஸ்ஸ ரணᾪர) (The Hon. Jayatissa Ranaweera) යුද්ධය නැති වුණාම දිනනවා තමයි. ගරු රවි කරුණානායක මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ரவி கᾞணாநாயக்க) (The Hon. Ravi Karunanayake) අපි බලමු. [බාධා කිරීමක්] ෙමතැන සහනාධාර ෙදන්න සල්ලි නැහැ කියා නැ ෙඟනහිර පළාත් සභාෙව් රුපියල් මිලියන 240ක් නාස්ති කරනවා. ඊට පස්ෙසේ සබරගමු පළාත් සභාවට රුපියල් මිලියන 220යි. ඊට පස්ෙසේ උතුරු මැද පෙද්ශයට රුපියල් මිලියන 240යි. ෙම්වා ඔක්ෙකොම දුන්නා ෙන්. නමුත් ඒ මුදලින් කිරි පැකට් එක රුපියල් 50 කින් අඩු කරන්න තිබුණා ෙන්. රුපියල් 80ට විකුණන්න පුළුවන් ෙපට්රල් ලීටර් එක දැන් ඛනිජ ෙතල් නීතිගත සංස්ථාෙව් විකුණන්ෙන් රුපියල් 157යි. ඇයි? ඇමතිවරු එකසිය නව ෙදෙනක් තියා ෙගන ඉන්න නිසායි. ඒ ඇමතිවරු එකසිය නවය රකින්න ෙපට්රල් ලීටරය රුපියල් 157ට විකුණනවා. කරුණාකර, - [බාධා කිරීමක්] ගරු මන්තීවරෙයක් (மாண்ᾗமிகு உᾠப்பினர் ஒᾞவர்) (An Hon. Member) ඇඟ තිබුණාට ෙමොළය නැහැ. ගරු රවි කරුණානායක මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ரவி கᾞணாநாயக்க) (The Hon. Ravi Karunanayake) ඇඟ ඔක්ස්ෆර්ඩ් ෙමොළය ෙමොන්ටිෙසෝරි තමයි. අපට කරන්න පුළුවන් වන්ෙන් ෙමොනවාද?

8 - PL 003040 - (2008/06)

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව 631 632

ෙම් රෙට් මුදල් ෙකොමිසමක් තිෙබනවා නම් අද උද්ධමනය සියයට 33ක් තිෙබනවායැ. ඉන්දියාව වා ෙග් රටක උද්ධමනය සියයට 8.5ක තියා ෙගන ඉන්න අවස්ථාෙව්දී ඇයි ලංකාෙව් විතරක් සියයට 33ක තිෙබන්ෙන්? ඒ වා ෙග්ම, අද ෙම් රෙට් බැංකු අයිරා ෙපොලිය සියයට 32යි. සියයට 32ක් කියන්ෙන් වɕාපාරයක් ෙගන යන්න පුළුවන් ෙපොලී පමාණයක්ද? අහිංසක පුද්ගලෙයක් ගිහිල්ලා නිවාස ණයක් ගන්නවා. එදා එක්සත් ජාතික පක්ෂ රජය කාලෙය් සියයට පෙහේ ෙපොලියට, සියයට හෙය් ෙපොලියට ණය අරගත්තත්, අද ගන්නා ණයවලට සියයට 32ක ෙපොලියක් ෙගවන්න සිදු ෙවලා තිෙබනවා. ඒවා ෙගවන්න පුළුවන් වන්ෙන් ෙකොයි ආකාරෙයන්ද? අද "ණය ෙගවන්න බැහැ" කියා නිවාස නැවත බැංකුවලට භාර ෙදනවා. ෙම් වාෙග් අපරාධයක්! දැන් විෙද්ශ කටයුතු ඇමතිත් ෙමතැනට ඇවිත් තිෙබනවා. ඔබතුමාෙග් මානව අයිතිවාසිකම් අනුව UN seat එකත් නැති ෙවලා තිෙබනවා. ඊට පස්ෙසේ කියනවා, අපි 100ක් දින්නා කියා. හරි වැඩක් ෙන්. ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama) 101ක්. ගරු රවි කරුණානායක මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ரவி கᾞணாநாயக்க) (The Hon. Ravi Karunanayake) 101ක්. ෙමොනවා දුන්නත් පුටුව අයින් ෙවලා තිෙබනවා. මානව අයිතිවාසිකම් සම්බන්ධෙයන් කරන්ෙන් ෙමොනවාද කියා අපි අහනවා. දයාන් ජයතිලක කරන පකාශ අමාතɕතුමා අනුමත කරනවාද? දයාන් ජයතිලක එෙහ ශබ්ද කරනවා. බිතානɕෙය් තානාපති ෙගනැවිත් විෙද්ශ අමාතɕාංශයට ගිහින් කියනවා, "කනගාටුයි, කියපු ෙද් ගැන" කියා. ෙම්වා පසිද්ධ කරන්ෙන් නැත්ෙත් ඇයි? අපි අහනවා. අමාතɕතුමා සමාවක් ඉල්ලුෙව් නැද්ද - ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama) විනාඩියක් ෙදන්න. තමුන්නාන්ෙසේ ෙම්වා කථා කිරීම ගැන මම ඉතාමත් සන්ෙතෝෂ ෙවනවා. අපි තානාපති ෙසේවෙය් සියලුම ෙද්වල් සම්බන්ධෙයන් කථා කිරීෙම්දී පසිද්ධිෙය් කළ යුතු ෙද්වල් පසිද්ධිෙය් ෙනොකළ යුතු ෙද්වල් තිෙබනවා. ඒ අනුව තමයි අෙප් විෙද්ශ වැඩ පිළිෙවළවල් කර ෙගන යන්ෙන්. ගරු රවි කරුණානායක මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ரவி கᾞணாநாயக்க) (The Hon. Ravi Karunanayake) ඒක තමයි. ගෙම් චණ්ඩියා වාෙග් දයාන් ජයතිලක ජිනීවාවල කෑ ගහන්න පුළුවන්. - ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama) නමුත් තමුන්නාන්ෙසේට ෙහොඳ දැනුමක් තිෙබනවා කියන්න පුළුවන්, ෙම් ඇතුෙළේ ෙකෙරන ෙද්වල් ගැන. ගරු රවි කරුණානායක මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ரவி கᾞணாநாயக்க) (The Hon. Ravi Karunanayake) ගෙම් චණ්ඩියා වා ෙග් එෙහේ කෑ ගහන්න පුළුවන්. ෙමෙහ ෙගනැල්ලා අෙන් අෙප් කනගාටුව පකාශ කරනවා කියලා කියනවා. විලි ලජ්ජාවක් නැහැ. කකුල් ෙදෙකන් හිට ෙගන කියන්න. රට ෙවනුෙවන් සමාවක් ඉල්ලන්න. ඒ වාෙග් අනිසි

පකාශ කරන තස්තවාදියා තමයි දහතුන්වන සංෙශෝධනය පාවිච්චි කරලා ඊළමක් ඉල්ලුෙව්. තව කවුද? අන්න ඒ ෙගොල්ලන් තමයි සිංහල ෙකොටිෙයො කියන්ෙන්. දැන් ඒ ෙගොල්ලන් ජීනීවා ගිහින් ශබ්ද කරනවා. Are you accepting what he said about the monarchy. Why do you not make a public apology? ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama) Are you making a point about our Geneva representative? Appropriate action will be taken regarding that matter. ගරු රවි කරුණානායක මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ரவி கᾞணாநாயக்க) (The Hon. Ravi Karunanayake) I know, it is not your representative. But, unfortunately, he has been appointed a representative. I know your style. But, what to do? Gunasekara is also listening. I know he will at least try to do something. Ensure that you stand up. Get the Seventeenth Amendment put into place. Look at the Hon. G.L. Peiris. We have already cleaned it up. ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama)

[ගරු රවි කරුණානායක මහතා]

2008 ජුනි 19 637 638

[අ.භා.4.02] ගරු එන්. ශී කාන්තා මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு என். ᾯ காந்தா) (The Hon. N. Srikantha) Mr. Deputy Speaker, I am very happy to participate in this Debate at its tail end on behalf of the Tamil National Alliance. In fact, Sir, having observed the proceedings in regard to this Debate right from its inception, I have been able to see that there have been serious deviations on the part of most of the speakers from both sides of this House from the very matter that is at the core of this Adjournment Motion moved by the Hon. Joseph Michael Perera. I would like to deal with the Motion confining myself, Sir, to the parameters of his very wordings so that, I do believe, I would be able to do justice to the topic that is in my hands now. It has been stated by some speakers on behalf of the Government and more particularly by my Good Friend, the Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama, the Foreign Minister, that since a Select Committee has already been appointed in July, 2006 to go into the shortcomings of the Seventeenth Amendment and also the necessary improvements and amendments needed for its effective operation, if I have understood him correctly - I do believe that I have understood the Hon. Minister correctly as I used to do always whenever it comes to him - there is no duty cast upon the President and by extension on the Government headed by His Excellency the President to appoint the Constitutional Council. I have always found the Hon. Foreign Minister coming out with very sound arguments whenever he used to hold the Floor on behalf of the Government. But I am rather disappointed, I say with due respect to my Hon. Friend, that this occasion, in fact, has been a very rare exception in that regard. The Hon. Foreign Minister stated that the Select Committee has been going into this. This House has agreed to appoint a Select Committee; the proceedings are not yet over, therefore, according to him, we have to wait for the outcome of the proceedings of the Select Committee, for its findings to act upon it. Sir, on behalf of the Tamil National Alliance, I say that we reject flatly this argument advanced on behalf of the Government. There is no point, Sir, in dealing with the Seventeenth Amendment separately as if it is of a separate, distinct and independent existence away from the Constitution itself. The Seventeenth Amendment is indeed part and parcel of the Constitution. I do not think there would be any dispute when I say that when an amendment has been proposed to the Constitution and after due deliberations and debate, passed by this House with a two-thirds majority as mandated by the self-fame Constitution and certified in accordance with the Constitution, it is incorporated into the Constitution and becomes an inseparable part of it. According to this portion of the Constitution, namely what we have in the form of the Seventeenth Amendment, or in other words, as far as the

Constitution, duly amended by the Seventeenth Amendment, stands today, there cannot be any shirking of duty on the part of His Excellency the President in appointing the Constitutional Council or constituting the Constitutional Council when nominations under Article 41A(e) and (f) are received by him. That is, in other words, when five persons are nominated together by the Prime Minister and the Leader of the Opposition and also another Member as agreed between the political parties and the independent groups other than the parties to which the Prime Minister and the Leader of the Opposition belong to respectively to be the members of the Constitutional Council, it is the duty of His Excellency the President to constitute the Constitutional Council. There cannot be any other interpretation that can be accorded to Article 41A of the Constitution as it stands today amended by the Seventeenth Amendment. But, what has happened in this instance? There is no Constitutional Council just because the House had agreed in July, 2006 to have a Select Committee. The Select Committee so appointed is still going on, the Government ranks trot out the defence that they are not duty-bound to rush into constituting the Constitutional Council; in other words, the President need not rush into constituting the Constitutional Council. I beg to state, Sir, let us not play politics with the Constitutional Council. I am not treating this Constitution as if it is a sacred document. It is a Constitution that was promulgated in 1978 by the so-called political genius, who was also known as a political “jackal”, I do not mean any disrespect, former President Junius Richard Jayewardene as if it is bound to be there and we all are bound by that. I am not saying that. Because this Constitution was framed, put into place and promulgated without the participation of the duly elected Representatives of our people, who were at that time represented by the Tamil United Liberation Front, which is one of the constituent members of our Tamil National Alliance today, the Tamil people rejected this Constitution. That is a different matter altogether. We have a Constitution and under this Constitution, we have this House, this august Assembly and we all are Members of this august Assembly and therefore, we are expected to play the game in accordance with the rules. If we play football, we have to play football as it is football. If we are going to play rugby or rugger, as it is known, it is entirely a different proposition altogether. Here, we have the Constitution and under the Constitution, we have this august Assembly duly elected and duly constituted. We have the Office of the President or the Presidency as a Constitutional institution. But we find that there is an adamant refusal and atrocious disregard in implementing what is mandated under the Constitution in regard to the Constitutional Council. It is a very serious matter. It is a very serious matter, Sir, because the Constitutional Council is no joke. The Constitutional Council has been granted immense powers, in that, it is involved even in regard to the appointment of the Chief Justice and other

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව

[ගරු එන්. ශී කාන්තා මහතා]

Judges of the Supreme Court; it is concerned under the Constitution with the appointment of the President and the other Judges of the Court of Appeal. What has happened now? We have had appointments made to the Supreme Court without the approval of the Constitutional Council because there was no Constitutional Council. We have had appointments made to the Court of Appeal and those judges are functioning as Judges of the Court of Appeal and those appointments have been made without the approval of the Constitutional Council for the simple reason that there was no Constitutional Council. Sir, as I told you at the very outset, confining myself to the parameters of the topic that is in my hands at this moment, I would like to quote Article 41C of the Seventeenth Amendment to the Constitution. “No person shall be appointed by the President to any of the Offices specified in the Schedule to this Article, unless such appointment has been approved by the Council upon a recommendation made to the Council by the President.” Now I would read out the Schedule, Part I. It states as follows: I quote: “ (a) The Chief Justice and the Judges of the Supreme Court (b) The President and the Judges of the Court of Appeal (c ) The Members of the Judicial Service Commission other than the Chairman” And there is Part II also. I am not going into that. Now Mr. Deputy Speaker, if a citizen of this country goes before the Supreme Court and says that a particular Judge of the Supreme Court cannot hold office for the simple reason that his appointment by His Excellency the President was not approved by the Constitutional Council, what would be the outcome? By the same logic and by the same argument, if another citizen goes before the Supreme Court and challenges the appointment of a particular Judge of the Court of Appeal who has been so appointed without the approval of the Constitutional Council, what would be the ensuing scenario? I am very sorry, Mr. Deputy Speaker, that a constitutional crisis is being fomented by the adamant attitude that has been exhibited by the Government in this regard. If such a situation arises and a challenge is thrown in regard to the appointments of some of the Judges of the Supreme Court who have been so appointed and also some of the Judges of the Court of Appeal who have been so appointed, I am rather sad to state that there will be a constitutional confrontation between the Government, or rather the Executive including His Excellency the President on the one hand and the judiciary on the other. There will be a constitutional confrontation ultimately leading to a constitutional crisis and eventually making way for a constitutional deadlock. I wish the Government and its Head, His Excellency the President, would take a serious note of this.

What happened in Pakistan recently? There has been a vibrant judiciary headed by an aggressively independent Chief Justice and an alert unofficial bar, which is still agitating for the constitutional rights of the people of Pakistan. We have witnessed enough in Pakistan. It might have been Pakistan yesterday, it is Pakistan today and I wonder whether it would be Sri Lanka tomorrow. Therefore, let us not play with the very creator of all these institutions, including this august Assembly of which all of us are Members. If the creation tries to be funny with the creator the end result would be very unfortunate. I do believe, Mr. Deputy Speaker, according to our own mythology - not that I am a believer of mythology but I am only quoting - there are quite a good number of instances of the creation having been funny with the creator and ended up with something very unfortunate. Let us not play political games. I am rather sorry to state that even from this side irrelevant matters were trotted out. I expected the Opposition to be very sharp and be straight in their arguments in relation to this Bill. There are matters that may be incidental to the Bill and now we would have occasion to deal with them. Here I wonder whether the Government is conscious of what is in stock. If there is a crisis, I think all those who are involved would be answerable - if not today, if not tomorrow, some day in future - because the offices they hold are in fact the creations of this Constitution. Mr. Deputy Speaker, having said that, I would like to deal with another aspect of this matter. That is where I really started. The fact that the select committee, which is going into any possibility of incorporating improvements in order to deal with any insufficiencies that are there, has nothing to do with the issue that is before us. Let us remember that no article of the Constitution, no chapter of the Constitution or for that matter, no part of the Constitution can be suspended even for a fraction of a second by the appointment of any number of select committees. There can be any number of select committees comprising of any number of honourables - I say that without any disrespect to anyone of us or anyone of them there. There can be any number of select committees consisting of any number of honourables, but no select committee can have the power, can arrogate to itself the power to suspend the Constitution, because the Constitution is the basis and the bedrock of the democratic functioning of this country; of the system of governance in this country. It is the very basis of all what we have in the name of law and order. It is the very basis of all what we have in regard to the institutions of governance. A select committee can go into that. This House has the power to appoint such a select committee. But that cannot put a break to the ever functioning constitutional mechanism. The Constitution is a living document. It is in black and white. I would not agree with this article or that article. I would rather like to see this Constitution be

replaced by another constitution that recognizes the principles of equality in full measure, that recognizes the principle of the right to self-determination of the different peoples of this country including the Tamil- speaking people. That is another matter. But, the fact that the Constitution cannot be tampered with, no article of the Constitution can be wished away, should not be lost sight of; is the message that I would like to register today on the Floor of this august Assembly - that too is a creation of this Constitution. But, as if the appointment of the select committee has suspended the Seventeenth Amendment to the Constitution, or rather halted the operation of the Seventeenth Amendment, or in other words the appointment of the select committee has suspended the relevant articles of the Constitution that mandate the constitution of the Constitutional Council by His Excellency the President - I do believe or I am rather sad to state that the Government is, in fact, groping in the dark. With the numerical strength the Government has, the Government Members may say this and that. But when it comes to a constitutional test, when it comes to a trial of strength in pure constitutional terms, I do believe, Mr. Deputy Speaker, that it is the Constitution that matters and it is only the Constitution that matters and the number in regard to one side or the numerical strength this side has, would be totally irrelevant. That is exactly why, Mr. Deputy Speaker, I would like to impress upon the Hon. Members of the Government ranks, including the Hon. Ministers who are here or who have rather been responsible to ensure their presence on behalf of the Government today in the ongoing Debate, to understand this issue very clearly. There is a proverb in my own sweet Tamil language, that a dutiful wife should act as a dutiful friend, as a good minister and also as a good counsellor. I expect at least some of the responsible Members of the Government to play that role in dealing with His Excellency the President. I wish that they would impress upon His Excellency the President that there is an impending crisis in this regard. A crisis is in the offing. That is, the nucleus is already there. The seeds have already been sown. They only have to germinate. If this matter is taken before the Supreme Court - please remember, we have a Chief Justice who is quite bold, independent minded and also have proven himself as one who would never hesitate to act if there is a necessity to act. If this matter is taken before the Supreme Court I think, the Government has to face the music. Let us stop living in our own dreamy lands. It is easy to live so, quite easy to live so. Come and sit here and just go on floating in the air as everything is permanent. People who had been adorning the front ranks of the Government a few years back are in political oblivion now. That is politics. Nothing is permanent.

We find the former President - I do say so with due respect to that fair lady whom I still find as very fair and attractive - lamenting now for the three mistakes that she has made in her political career while holding the office of Presidency and she is spelling out only two and reserving the third for a more opportune moment. I do not want that to happen to anybody else in this country. Mr. Deputy Speaker, even to fight the war, I think, the Government can act only in accordance with the Constitution. Nobody can go beyond the four walls of the Constitution; go beyond the parameters of the Constitution. There is no question of anybody subverting the Constitution from within. There cannot be anybody, however mighty he or she may be, tampering with the Constitution while being the creation of the very Constitution. නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමා (பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கள்) (The Deputy Speaker) Thank you, Hon. Member. ගරු එන්. ශී කාන්තා මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு என். ᾯ காந்தா) (The Hon. N. Srikantha) Having said that, I would like to conclude by saying that the Government and the Head of the Government, His Excellency the President, should do a rethinking on the matter and rise to the occasion, leaving aside meaningless pride and trivial political consideration and act in accordance with the Constitution. I thank you, Mr. Deputy Speaker.

නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමා (பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கள்) (The Deputy Speaker) Thank you. ගරු මහින්ද සමරසිංහ අමාතɕතුමා. ඔබතුමාට විනාඩි 15ක කාලයක් තිෙබනවා. [අ.භා. 4.29] ගරු මහින්ද සමරසිංහ මහතා (ආපදා කළමනාකරණ හා මානව හිමිකම් අමාතɕතුමා)

(மாண்ᾗமிகு மஹிந்த சமரசிங்க - அனர்த்த ᾙகாைமத்ᾐவ, மனித உாிைமகள் அைமச்சர்) (The Hon. Mahinda Samarasinghe - Minister of Disaster Management and Human Rights) Hon. Deputy Speaker, to avoid repetition, I would like to seek your permission, to table* the text of my speech because there is a lot of history that I have gone into and I do not want to repeat that because some Members have already mentioned that in the course of their speeches. But, I would like to deal with two or three salient points which I have incorporated in the text of this speech.

641 642

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව

[ගරු මහින්ද සමරසිංහ මහතා] ]

I could not agree more with the Hon. Srikantha when he said some Members have spoken to the point and others have brought as usual various other issues using the time allotted for this very important Debate. I was one of those Members of Parliament who were involved right from the inception when this Seventeenth Amendment to the Constitution was formulated. In fact, in 2001, I was the Deputy Whip of the Opposition and I can remember it was only at about 6.30 or 7.00 in the night that we brokered the deal, I mean, an agreement was reached between the Opposition and the Government, to put it for vote on a particular day. Negotiations lasted for many days and even for a few weeks, Sir, and of course it culminated on the day when the Seventeenth Amendment was to be taken up for vote and the Government wanted to have the two-thirds, as per the Constitution, to adopt this very important piece of legislation. We were negotiating, as I mentioned earlier, till about 7.00 in the night and finally we came to an agreement. I can remember it was the Hon. Wimal Weerawansa on the side of the Government and I on the side of the UNP who were the conduits for the two sides. Also, I can remember at 6.30 in the night going to the Prime Minister’s office and sitting down with him because there was an amendment that we wanted to be incorporated. He agreed to it. Then, I took it to the Hon. Ranil Wickremasinghe and the UNP agreed. That was how the two-thirds was put together. Sir, with that kind of a rushed last minute agreement being hammered out, there were bound to be lacunas, bound to be shortcomings and it is these shortcomings that we are trying to rectify by way of the Parliamentary Select Committee that the Hon. Dew Gunasekara is chairing. There again, Sir, it was my Motion to this Parliament that was adopted unanimously by the Hon. Members of Parliament on that side including the Hon. Srikantha. I brought the Motion before Parliament as the Minister of Human Rights because I recognized at that time that there were serious lacunas, serious shortcomings in the Seventeenth Amendment. I felt that we should give thought to rectifying these shortcomings once and for all and that is how the Select Committee was formulated and the Hon. Dew Gunasekara, Minister of Constitutional Affairs was asked to chair that. Now, Sir, the shortcomings, of course, were evident even before this whole hiatus of the Constitutional Council after March 2005 came about. The first was, when the Election Commission was to be appointed there was a nominee which the Constitutional Council had decided upon and the then President did not make that appointment. Of course, she gave various reasons as to why she was not going to make that appointment and there was no provision in the Seventeenth Amendment to ensure that a selection procedure which had been gone into by the Constitutional Council and the name decided upon, and when the name was sent to the President that the President has to act within a certain time period. That

was a shortcoming which we noticed even before the second Constitutional Council was going to be appointed. That was also something which had to be gone into and now the Select Committee, I believe, has gone into that and there is a recommendation in the Interim Report which the Hon. Dew Gunasekara will be presenting shortly. This would bring in a new Clause where there would be a certain time period within which the President has to act on the nomination of people as per the Schedules in the Seventeenth Amendment coming from the Constitutional Council. This is a big shortcoming which had to be rectified and this alone would have justified the rationale for the appointment of a Select Committee. Then, many of the Members stated in the course of the Debate, as to what happened post-March 2005. I have gone into it in great detail in the text of my speech tabled and I do not want to go into that again. We all know that it was neither the fault of His Excellency the President nor the Leader of the Opposition. The smaller parties in this Parliament could not come to an agreement on the nomination of a suitable candidate and this went on for several months. Only after a considerable period was spent, nearly two years, finally all of you came to a decision and nominated a person to be appointed. ගරු මාෛව ෙසෝ. ෙසේනාධිරාජා මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு மாைவ. ேசா. ேசனாதிராஜா) (The Hon. Mavai S. Senathirajah) Since then, about eight months have passed. ගරු මහින්ද සමරසිංහ මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு மஹிந்த சமரசிங்க) (The Hon. Mahinda Samarasinghe) I know. That is another shortcoming because when you have a provision in the Constitution for consensus to be reached within smaller parties, or for that matter, any political party represented in this Parliament, we know with the very charged atmosphere in which politics is done in this country that it is impossible at a practical level to come to a consensus. ගරු එන්. ශීකාන්තා මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு என். ᾯகாந்தா) (The Hon. N. Srikantha) Hon. Minister, will you permit me to intervene for a moment? ගරු මහින්ද සමරසිංහ මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு மஹிந்த சமரசிங்க) (The Hon. Mahinda Samarasinghe) Yes. ගරු එන්. ශීකාන්තා මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு என். ᾯகாந்தா) (The Hon. N. Srikantha) Once the nominations are made including that of the representative of the minor parties, the ball rolls into the court of the President. Then, the President has to act. He

643 644

2008 ජුනි 19

cannot shirk his responsibility. Our grievance is this. Now, the nominations have been made, but the Constitutional Council has not been constituted. But the President has appointed persons to hold offices mentioned in the Schedule. ගරු මහින්ද සමරසිංහ මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு மஹிந்த சமரசிங்க) (The Hon. Mahinda Samarasinghe) Hon. Srikantha, I was coming to that. I was going to explain as to why the Select Committee is important because do not forget that this House unanimously agreed to the Motion that I presented for the appointment of a Parliamentary Select Committee. Parliament is sovereign. His Excellency the President cannot usurp the powers of Parliament. He does not wish to do that. There are many shortcomings in this Seventeenth Amendment and that is why it is important that we deliberate together in an objective manner, in a manner of flexibility, in a manner of give-and-take, and for goodness' sake finalize the Select Committee process and bring the Report before Parliament. The Hon. Dew Gunasekara is waiting for consensus to be reached in this House. ගරු එන්. ශීකාන්තා මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு என். ᾯகாந்தா) (The Hon. N. Srikantha) Hon. Minister, suspend the working of the – ගරු මහින්ද සමරසිංහ මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு மஹிந்த சமரசிங்க) (The Hon. Mahinda Samarasinghe) I gave in to you. Let me finish my contribution. I did not disturb you. Now, Sir, there was also a question about as to whether the President had acted ultra vires to the Constitution in stepping in and making the appointments. I do not know whether the Hon. Srikantha is aware that there was an advice given by the Attorney-General that it is within the powers of His Excellency the President to make these appointments. I do not know whether the Hon. Srikantha is aware that the Appeal Court of Sri Lanka delivered a judgment to say that the President had acted intra vires, not ultra vires, to the Constitution in making these appointments. Now I can give you one example. ගරු එන්. ශීකාන්තා මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு என். ᾯகாந்தா) (The Hon. N. Srikantha) නැඟී සිටිෙය්ය. எᾨந்தார். rose. ගරු මහින්ද සමරසිංහ මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு மஹிந்த சமரசிங்க) (The Hon. Mahinda Samarasinghe) Hon. Srikantha, please wait. Please listen to me. - [Interruption.] Can you please let me speak? -[Interruption.] That, you go and sort out with the Appeal Court.

Now, I will give you one example, Hon. Srikantha, about the Human Rights Commission of Sri Lanka which is an institution dear to you and me both, as well as the Hon. Dew Gunasekara. There are five Commissioners who are to be appointed as Commissioners of the Human Rights Commission of Sri Lanka. Now, Sir, when you look at the Human Rights Commission of Sri Lanka Act and when you look at the powers and functions of the Commissioners in addition to the Commission, you would see that there are specific powers which are given to the Commissioners. For example, you cannot serve summons unless it is under the signature of the Chairman of the Human Rights Commission of Sri Lanka. If there is no Chairman, summons cannot be served. So, how do you discharge the mandate of the Human Rights Commission of Sri Lanka?

Then, Sir, the communication of a Certificate to the Supreme Court under Section 21 (4) of the Human Rights Commission of Sri Lanka Act, No. 21 of 1996 on contempt, is once again a function that cannot take place if the Commissioners are not in place. Recommendations after the investigations are completed cannot be made unless the Commissioners come into it and make the recommendations. Sir, we know how important the Human Rights Commission is for the general public of this country. If the Human Rights Commission is not functioning and if it has to function only with the officials but without the Commissioners, they would not be able to entertain, look into, investigate complaints, make recommendations, issue summons thereon and discharge their mandate. So, this is why His Excellency the President had to intervene and make these appointments. I am not afraid to say in this House that it would have been better if he had not done that because the ideal thing would have been to resort to the Constitutional Council mechanism. But at that point, there was no agreement among the smaller parties. It was only after that, the nomination was made. ගරු ඩිව් ගුණෙසේකර මහතා (ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථා හා ජාතික ඒකාබද්ධතා අමාතɕතුමා)

(மாண்ᾗமிகு ᾊᾝ குணேசகர - அரசியலைமப்ᾗ அᾤவல்கள், ேதசிய ஒᾞைமப்பாட்ᾌ அைமச்சர்) (The Hon. Dew Gunasekara -Minister of Constitutional Affairs and National Integration) That was in February, 2007. ගරු මහින්ද සමරසිංහ මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு மஹிந்த சமரசிங்க) (The Hon. Mahinda Samarasinghe) Yes. So, His Excellency the President had to intervene. Otherwise there would have been chaos. Therefore, please look at the background in which he has acted. He has not acted because he wants to manipulate the whole system. He has to run the country. He is the Head of State. We are the Government. We have to run this country. We cannot have a situation where none of these Commissions are functioning.

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව

Mahinda Samarasinghe) It has not been violated. It has been held. It has not been violated. - [Interruption.] Let me assure you that once Parliament adopts the final report of the Select Committee on the Seventeenth Amendment, it will be brought before the Cabinet and the Cabinet will consider the amendments that Parliament wishes it to consider. Of course, once the Government takes a decision on that, the relevant Hon. Minister will bring the amendments before this House. Then, all of us can come together and give our vote to ensure that these lacunas and shortcomings are eradicated once and for all. The other point is this, Sir. Everyone is talking about small parties, big parties, the President did not nominate or the Leader of the Opposition did not nominate, but if you want this Constitutional Council to be truly independent, do you think by having representatives nominated by the political parties in the Constitutional Council that it can ever take a decision independently? Do you think if the SLFP or the UNP or the TNA or the JVP or the SLMC or whatever other party that is represented in this Parliament nominates a person to be in the Constitutional Council, that that person is going to be truly independent and divorced of those political ideologies? No. We have to take the risk that those personalities who are nominated by the political parties may not be able to act independently. I am not pointing the finger at anyone in particular. But it can happen, Sir. Therefore, this whole thing has to be revisited. Are we going to allow political parties, Hon. Minister, to nominate personalities to this very important body, the Constitutional Council? Please look at it - ගරු එන්. ශීකාන්තා මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு என். ᾯகாந்தா) (The Hon. N. Srikantha) Hon. Minister, I say this with due respect to you. You are talking about what in your view is an ideal situation. We are concerned about what is here in black and white in the Constitution. ගරු මහින්ද සමරසිංහ මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு மஹிந்த சமரசிங்க) (The Hon. Mahinda Samarasinghe) Hon. We are now trying to get it right the second time round. ගරු එන්. ශීකාන්තා මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு என். ᾯகாந்தா) (The Hon. N. Srikantha) Hon. Minister, may I pose one more question? There are a lot of grievances in regard to the Constitution –

ගරු මහින්ද සමරසිංහ මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு மஹிந்த சமரசிங்க) (The Hon. Mahinda Samarasinghe) Hon. Srikantha, please sit down and let me finish my speech. But if we are doing it, all I am saying is, Sir, let us do it properly. Thank you very much, Sir. *සභා ෙම්සය මත තබන ලද කථාව : சபாபீடத்தில் ைவக்கப்பட்ட உைர : Speach tabled: Address by the Hon Mahinda Samarasinghe MP Minister of Disaster Management and Human Rights on the occasion of the Adjournment Debate in Parliament on the Seventeenth Amendment to the Sri Lankan Constitution Sri Jayawardenepura– Kotte, 19 June 2008 Mr. Deputy Speaker, this debate on the Seventeenth Amendment to the Constitution is both timely and of great significance. The Seventeenth Amendment, which was certified on 03rd October 2001, wrought a fundamental change in the realm of constitutional governance in Sri Lanka. Since the 1990 s there had been a cry for reform of the system of appointment of certain public institutions and offices due to perceived politicization and partisan bias in the appointment of these institutions and offices. These institutions and offices, Mr. Speaker, were no ordinary departments, boards or bureaus of Government. They were vital national institutions that, by their very nature and responsibilities, should have commanded the utmost confidence of all Sri Lankans. Any perception of political influence, partisanship or bias could damage the confidence, trust and faith reposed in them. In the event that this had happened, the consequences for our system of democratic Governance could have been drastic. It was felt at the time that added assurances of their independence, impartiality and integrity should be made. The Seventeenth Amendment was the best possible answer that the Legislature could provide. The first Constitutional Council appointed under the Seventeenth Amendment was constituted in March 2002. Its term of office therefore expired in March 2005. It is a matter of historical record that a problem arose due to the lack of consensus among eligible numerically smaller parties in Parliament as to the tenth member of the Council who would be nominated by these parties and appointed by the President. Since all ten members were not appointed,

647 648

2008 ජුනි 19

the Council could not commence functioning. This was not merely the view of the Government but was based on the advice of the then Attorney-General. The resulting deadlock was the creation of a situation that no fresh appointments to these critically important national institutions and offices could be made. In these circumstances the machinery of state and of Government was in danger of grinding to a complete halt. In these circumstances, His Excellency the President was compelled to make some appointments due to the fact that the Constitutional Council was not constituted. It is the view of the Government that the appointment to these national institutions and offices was of such critical significance and that their existence and functioning was of such great importance that the President was fully justified in using his residuary executive power under the Constitution to make these appointments. The question of the President’s residuary powers being exercised in analogous circumstances has been held to be intra vires the Constitution by the courts of Sri Lanka. Mr. Deputy Speaker, take, for instance, the Human Rights Commission of Sri Lanka. If the appointments of the five Commissioners were not made, the Commission would cease to function as an effective institution. In these circumstances the staff of the Commission, the ordinary petitioners who sought relief, the pending matters before the Commission all could not function or be proceeded with. It is not only a question of the five individuals who were to be appointed as Commissioners. It is a question of an eleven-year old institution of State being rendered non-functional. In the absence of Commissioners the issuance of summons, recommendations of the Commission, the communication of a Certificate to the Supreme Court under section 21(4) of the act on contempt are among the functions that cannot take place in terms of the Human Rights Commission Act, No 21 of 1996. However, Mr. Deputy Speaker, these domestic legal and Constitutional questions do have repercussions outside our shores. The International. Co-ordinating Committee of National Human Rights Institutions (ICC) has downgraded the Human Rights Commission from Grade “A” (member) to “B” (observer) status. One of the reasons attributed was the nonconformity of the appointment process with the Paris Principles relating to the status of national institutions. These Principles were adopted by the former UN Human Rights Commission in 1992 and the UN General Assembly in 1993. The Human Rights Commission of Sri Lanka is now relegated to observer status by the ICC due to non-conformity. This is not to say that the Human Rights Commission has lost its independence. Indeed no-one has cast any aspersions against the Commissioners or the Commission on this score. However the deadlock over the Seventeenth Amendment has affected the recognition accorded to the Commission internationally. This creates a less than favourable image of Sri Lanka. The Seventeenth Amendment is a key factor in our response for repeated calls for the establishment in Sri Lanka of an Office of the UN High Commissioner for Human Rights to perform a monitoring cum reporting function. I have constantly reiterated the Government’s consolidated position that we possess the institutional framework to promote and protect human rights. This framework includes an independent Human Rights Commission. We have said that an office of the OHCHR is not necessary in these circumstances. Our argument has been that we need to further strengthen our national institutions and that we require technical assistance and capacity building support from our international partners to strengthen then institutions to perform all functions necessary to uphold and safeguard human rights. Our position, Mr. Deputy Speaker, will be greatly strengthened if we are able to demonstrate that institutions such as the Human Rights Commission are constituted in accordance with the constitutional provisions of the Seventeenth Amendment. International interest in the Seventeenth Amendment is not limited to the Human Rights Commission alone. Mr. Deputy Speaker, in the recently concluded Universal Periodic Review of Sri Lanka at the UN Human Rights Council in Geneva, many member countries expressed their wish to see the reconstitution - of the Constitutional Council as a re-assurance of the independence of the Judicial service Commission, the Police Commission and other vital national institutions. This is not the first time that such pronouncements have been made at international fora. We have consistently taken the position –at the Human Rights Council in Geneva and elsewhere—that Sri Lanka has set in motion a process to renew and reinvigorate the Seventeenth Amendment and that we are committed to continuing to

work towards this goal. It was with the intention of initiating definite action on rectifying the deficiencies in the Seventeenth Amendment, that I proposed the establishment of the Parliamentary Select Committee to look into the operation of the Seventeenth Amendment to the Constitution. My resolution was unanimously endorsed by this august Assembly. The Committee, under the able stewardship of my colleague the Hon. Minister of Constitutional Affairs and National Integration, has formulated an interim report containing detailed recommendations for consideration by this House. The Select Committee has had wide ranging consultations and has, I believe addressed the core issues in a spirit of good faith, pragmatism and common-sense. His Excellency the President has expressed his confidence in the Legislature’s ability to formulate a set of proposals for amendment of the Seventeenth Amendment and has assured that, once Parliament adopts and endorses the findings and recommendations of the Select Committee, he will be prepared to bring the required amendments before Cabinet for its consideration. I trust that the Select Committee will be able to address its mind to the draft report and submit a final consensus document to this House. I am certain that we will, through concerted effort and active co-operation, be able to provide a solution to the problems created by the Seventeenth Amendment. Mr. Deputy Speaker, as stated before, the national institutions mentioned in the Schedule to Article 41B and the offices mentioned in the Schedule to Article 41C contained in Chapter VIIA of the Constitution, are vital components of our national institutional framework. Our honest and sincere efforts must be directed towards ensuring that the sovereign people of Sri Lanka continue to hold these institutions in high regard. The future of our system of democratic governance could well rely on this continued confidence. We must, from this point forward, dedicate ourselves to ensuring the smooth functioning of the Seventeenth Amendment - an integral and essential part of the Constitution of Sri Lanka. Thank you, Mr. Speaker. නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමා (பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கள்) (The Deputy Speaker) Thank you. ගරු නිෙයෝජɕ කාරක සභාපති රාමලිංගම් චන්දෙසේකර් මැතිතුමා. [பி.ப.4.46] ගරු රාමලිංගම් චන්දෙසේකර් මහතා (නිෙයෝජɕ කාරක සභාපතිතුමා) (மாண்ᾗமிகு இரா. சந்திரேசகர் - குᾨக்களின் பிரதித் தவிசாளர்)

(The Hon. Ramalingam Chandrasekar - Deputy Chairman of Committees) ெகளரவ பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கேள, அரசியலைமப்ᾗக்கான பதிேனழாவᾐ திᾞத்தத்ைத அᾙல்பᾌத்த நடவᾊக்ைக எᾌக்காைம ெதாடர்பான இந்த ஒத்திைவப்ᾗ விவாதத்தில் எனக்கும் ஒᾞசில வார்த்ைதகள் ேபசுவதற்குச் சந்தர்ப்பம் அளித்தைதயிட்ᾌ எனᾐ நன்றிையத் ெதாிவித்ᾐக் ெகாள்கின்ேறன். அரசியலைமப்ᾗக்கான பதிேனழாவᾐ திᾞத்தச் சட்டத்தில் சில ஆைணக்குᾨக்கைள அைமப்பதற்கான ᾙன்ெமாழிᾫகள் ெசய்யப்பட்ᾊᾞப்பᾐம், அᾐ சம்பந்தமான விமர்சனங்கᾦம் கண்டனங்கᾦம் இந்த சைபயில் ஒᾢத்ᾐக் ெகாண்ᾊᾞப்பᾐம் உங்கᾦக்குத் ெதாிᾜம். மக்கள் விᾌதைல ᾙன்னணியினராகிய நாங்கள் இந்த அரசியலைமப் ᾗக்கான பதிேனழாவᾐ திᾞத்தச் சட்டத்ைத ஏன், எதற்காக உடனᾊயாக நைடᾙைறப்பᾌத்ᾐங்கள் என்ᾠ அரைசக் ேகட்கின்ேறாம் என்றால், ேவᾠ எதனாᾤமல்ல, இலங்ைகயில் பிறந்ᾐ, இலங்ைகயில் வாᾨகின்ற அைனத்ᾐ மக்கᾦம் இந்தப் பாராᾦமன்றத்ைத அதிᾜயர்சைப என்ᾠ கᾞᾐகின்ற அேதேநரம், இந்தப் பாராᾦமன்றத்திᾕடாக நிைறேவற்றப்பட்ᾊᾞக்கின்ற அரசியலைமப்ᾗச் சட்டத்ைத அதிᾜன்னதமான சட்டம் என்ᾠம் நம்ᾗவதனாᾤம்தான். ஆயிᾔம், அதிᾜன்னதமான சட்டம் என்ᾠ கᾞதப்பᾌகின்ற இந்தச் சட்டத்தில் ஏᾐம் பிைழகள் அல்லᾐ குைறபாᾌகள் இᾞக்கின்றனவா? அப்பᾊயாயின் அைவகைள

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව

[ගරු රාමලිංගම් චන්දෙසේකර් මහතා] ]

நிவர்த்தி ெசய்வᾐ எப்பᾊ? என்கின்ற வாதப்பிரதிவாதங்கள் ஒᾞᾗறᾙம் அᾐ சம்பந்தமான விமர்சனங்கள் மᾠᾗறᾙம் இᾞக்கத்தான் ெசய்கின்றன. ெகளரவ பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கேள, விேசடமாக இந்தப் பதிேனழாவᾐ அரசியலைமப்ᾗக்கான பதிேனழாவᾐ திᾞத்தச் சட்டம் பற்றி இன்ᾠ இலங்ைகயில் இᾞக்கின்ற அரசியல் கட்சிகள் மத்தியில் பல்ேவᾠவிதமான எதிர்பார்ப்ᾗக்கள் இᾞக்கின்றன. குறிப்பாகக் கூறினால், ேதர்தல் ஆைணக்குᾨ, ெபாᾢஸ் ஆைணக்குᾨ, அரச ேசைவ ஆைணக்குᾨ மற்ᾠம் நீதிச் ேசைவ ஆைணக்குᾨ ஆகியன சம்பந்தமாகப் பலᾞம் பலவிதமான எதிர்பார்ப்ᾗக்கᾦடேனேய இᾞக்கின்றனர். ெகளரவ பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கேள, இந்த எதிர்பார்ப்ᾗக்கேளாᾌ தமிழ்ெமாழி ேபசுகின்ற குᾊமகனான என்னால் அவதானிக்கக்கூᾊய பிரதான பிரச்சிைன ஒன்ᾠம் இᾞக்கின்றᾐ. அந்தப் பிரச்சிைனதான் இன்ᾠ இலங்ைகயில் தீர்க்கப்படாதிᾞக்கின்ற ேதசியப் பிரச்சிைன. அதனால்தான் நாங்கள் எல்ேலாᾞம் இந்த ேதசியப் பிரச்சிைன சம்பந்தமாக கூᾌதலாகப் ேபசுகின்ேறாம். இங்கு நாங்கள் ஜனநாயகத்ைதப் பற்றிப் ேபசுகின்ேறாம் ; அந்த ஜனநாயகத்தின் ஊடான சமத்ᾐவத்ைதப் பற்றிப் ேபசுகின்ேறாம். காரணம், அதன் ஊடாக இந்த நாட்ᾊல் ஒᾞ நல்லாட்சி ஏற்பᾌத்தப்பட ேவண்ᾌம் என்கின்ற ஆைச - ஆவல் இன்ᾠ அைனவᾞக்கும், அைனத்ᾐக் கட்சிகᾦக்கும் இᾞப்பதனால்தான். அப்பᾊயானால், நாங்கள் ᾙதᾢல் கூறியᾐேபால அதிᾜன்னத சட்டமான அரசியலைமப்ᾗச் சட்டத்தில் சாியான சரத்ᾐக்கள் உள்ளடங்கியிᾞக்கின்றனவா? என்ᾠ நாங்கள் ேதᾊப் பார்க்கேவண்ᾌம். இன்ᾠ இந்த நாட்ᾊல் ஆட்கடத்தல் மற்ᾠம் ெகாைல, ெகாள்ைள ேபான்ற பல்ேவᾠ சம்பவங்கள் நைடெபற்ᾠக்ெகாண்ᾊᾞக் கின்றன. இந்தச் சம்பவங்கᾦக்கு அரசாங்கம் ெபாᾠப்பா, இல்ைலயா? என்பதற்கு அரசாங்கம்தான் பதில் கூறியாக ேவண்ᾌம். ஏன் நாம் இவ்வாᾠ கூᾠகின்ேறாம் என்றால், அவ்வாᾠ கடத்தப்பᾌகின்ற நபர்கள், அவ்வாᾠ ைகᾐ ெசய்யப் பᾌகின்ற நபர்கள், அவ்வாᾠ காணாமல்ேபாகின்ற நபர்கள் ெதாடர்பாக அரசாங்கப் பக்கத்திᾢᾞந்ᾐ ெவட்டெவளிச்சமான, ெதளிவான கᾞத்ᾐக்கள் வᾞகின்றதா என்ᾠ நாம் ேதᾊப் பார்க்கின்றெபாᾨᾐ, அல்லᾐ இதற்கு உாிய தீர்ᾫ காணப்பட்டதா அல்லᾐ கடத்தப்பட்டவர்கள் எங்கு இᾞக்கின்றார்கள் அல்லᾐ ைகᾐ ெசய்யப்பட்டவர்கள் எங்கு இᾞக்கின்றார்கள், சித்திரவைதக் குள்ளானவர்கள் எங்கு இᾞக்கின்றார்கள்? என்ᾠ கண்ᾌபிᾊக்கப் பட்டதா என்ᾠ நாம் ேதᾊப் பார்க்கின்றெபாᾨᾐ, அைவ ேகள்விக்குறியாகேவ இᾞக்கின்றன. காணாமல் ேபானவர்கள் இன்னᾙம் காணாமல் ேபானவர்களாகேவ கᾞதப்பᾌகின்றார்கள். இதனால் இன்ᾠ இலங்ைக அரசாங்கம் மனித உாிைம மீறல்கள் சம்பந்தமாக சர்வேதச ாீதியாகக் கᾞம் ᾗள்ளிையப் ெபற்றிᾞக் கின்றᾐ. ெகளரவ பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கேள, இன்ᾠ மிக மிக ேவதைனக்குாிய விடயம் என்னெவன்றால், விேசடமாக “இலங்ைக என்பᾐ மனித உாிைமகள் மீறப்பᾌகின்ற ஒᾞ நாᾌ! இலங்ைக என்பᾐ தமிழர்கள் நிம்மதியாக வாழ ᾙᾊயாத ஒᾞ நாᾌ! இலங்ைகயானᾐ தமிழ் மக்கைளப் பᾌெகாைல ெசய்கின்ற ஒᾞ நாᾌ! அல்லᾐ அங்கிᾞப்பᾐ இவ்வாறான ஓர் அரசாங்கம்” என்கின்ற ஒᾞ கᾞத்ᾐ இன்ᾠ சா்வேதச ாீதியாக வியாபித் திᾞக்கின்றைமயாகும். இவ்வாᾠ சர்வேதசாீதியாக வியாபித்ᾐ இலங்ைகக்குப் பாாிய அபகீர்த்திையப் ெபற்ᾠக்ெகாᾌத்திᾞக் கின்ற இந்தக் கᾞத்ᾐக்கைள ெவளிநாᾌகᾦக்குக் ெகாண்ᾌ ெசல்கின்றவர்கᾦம் இந்த நாட்ᾊன் அரசியல்வாதிகளாகேவ இᾞக்கின்றார்கள் ; அᾐᾫம் மனவᾞத்தத்திற்குாிய ஒᾞ விடயமாக இᾞக்கின்றᾐ. அப்பᾊயானால் இந்தக் கᾞத்ᾐக்கைளத் ேதால்வியைடயச் ெசய்வதற்கு அல்லᾐ இந்தக் கᾞத்ᾐக்கைள மாற்றியைமப்பதற்கு அரசாங்கம் என்ன ெசய்திᾞக்கின்றᾐ? என்ᾠ நாங்கள் ேதᾊப் பார்க்கின்றெபாᾨᾐ ெகளரவ பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கேள, மிக, மிக ேவதைனக்குாிய விடயம் என்னெவன்றால், அரசாங்கத்திᾤள்ள 107 அைமச்சர்கᾦம் ேபச்சளவில் ெசயற்பᾌ

கின்றார்கேள தவிர ேவᾠ இல்ைல. இன்ᾠ குைறந்தபட்சம் இந்தியாவில் தமிழ் நாட்ᾊல் இலங்ைகக்கு ஏற்பட்ᾊᾞக்கின்ற அபகீர்த்திையப் ேபாக்குவதற்கு ஏᾐவான நடவᾊக்ைககளாவᾐ எᾌக்கப்பட்ᾊᾞக்கின்றனவா? என்ᾠ நாங்கள் ேதᾊப் பார்க்கின்ற ெபாᾨᾐ அᾐᾫம் இல்ைல. இன்ᾠ இலங்ைக அரசாங்கத்ைதப் பிரதிநிதித்ᾐவம் ெசய்கின்ற சில பிரதியைமச்சர்கள் அல்லᾐ அைமச்சர்கள் இந்தியாᾫக்குச் ெசன்ᾠ கூᾠகின்றார்கள், “இலங்ைக என்பᾐ தமிழ் மக்கள் வாழ ᾙᾊயாத ஒᾞ நாᾌ” என்ᾠ. ெகளரவ பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கேள, “இலங்ைகயில் தமிழர்கள் வாழ ᾙᾊயாததனால் உடனᾊயாக இந்தியா தைலயிட்ᾌத் தமிழ் மக்கைளப் பாᾐகாக்க ேவண்ᾌம்!” - இதைன நாங்கள் கூறவில்ைல, இன்ᾠ இந்த அரசாங்கத்தில் அைமச்சா்களாக, பிரதியைமச்சர்களாக இᾞக்கின்ற சிலேர இந்தியாவிᾤள்ள தமிழ் நாட்ᾊற்குச் ெசன்ᾠ இதைனக் கூᾠகின்றார்கள். ெகளரவ பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கேள, இந்த ஓலக்குரல் என்பᾐ இன்ᾠ ேநற்ᾠ அல்ல, கடந்த இᾞபᾐ வᾞடங்கᾦக்கு ேமலாக எமᾐ நாᾌ சம்பந்தமாகத் திணிக்கப் பட்ᾊᾞக்கின்ற கᾞத்ᾐ. அப்பᾊயானால் இᾐ ஒᾞ பாரᾑரமான நிைலைமயாகும். ஆகேவ, இந்தப் பாரᾑரமான நிைலைமையப் ேபாக்குவதற்கு இலங்ைகயின் அதிᾜயர் சட்டம் என்ᾠ கᾞதப்பᾌகின்ற இலங்ைகயின் அரசியலைமப்ᾗச் சட்டத்தில் என்ன வழிவைக ெசய்யப்பட்ᾊᾞக்கின்றᾐ என்பைத நாங்கள் ேதᾊப் பார்க்க ேவண்ᾌம். ெகளரவ பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கேள, “நாங்கள் அைனவᾞம் இலங்ைகயர்கள்! நாங்கள் அைனவᾞம் மனிதர்கள்! நாங்கள் அைனவᾞம் ஒᾞ ெகாᾊயின்கீழ் வாழேவண்ᾊய மக்கள்!” என்ᾠ இன்ᾠ கூᾠகின்ேறாம். தனிப்பட்ட ாீதியில் நாட்ᾊல் இᾞக்கின்ற அரசியல்வாதிகள் அைனவᾞைடய ஆவல் - ஆைச - அவா எல்லாம் இந்த நாட்ᾊல் தமிழ், சிங்கள, ᾙஸ்ᾢம் மக்கள் - ᾚவின மக்கᾦம் - ஒᾞ ெகாᾊயின்கீழ் ஒற்ᾠைமயாக வாழ்வதற்ேகற்றவைகயில் இந்த நாᾌ கட்ᾊெயᾨப்பப்பட ேவண்ᾌம் என்பதாகும். ஆனால், இலங்ைகயில் தமிழ்ெமாழி ேபசுகின்ற மக்கᾦக்குச் சமத்ᾐவம் வழங்கப்பட்ᾊᾞப்பதாகக் கூறப்பᾌகின்றேபாதிᾤம், இலங்ைகயின் அரசியலைமப்ᾗச் சட்டத்தில் "இலங்ைகயின் அரசகᾞமெமாழி சிங்களம்" என்ᾠ கூறப்பட்ᾊᾞப்பᾐடன் "தமிழ்ெமாழிᾜம் ஓர் அரசகᾞம ெமாழி யாகும்" என்ற பதம் ேசர்க்கப்பட்ᾊᾞக்கின்றᾐ. நான் ᾙன்னர் கூறியᾐேபால் நாங்கள் அைனவᾞம் ஒᾞ தாய் மக்கள் எனில், எதற்காக அரசியலைமப்ᾗச் சட்டத்தில் "சிங்களெமாழி அரச கᾞம ெமாழி" என்ᾠ குறிப்பிட்ᾌவிட்ᾌ, "தமிழ்ெமாழிᾜம் ஓர் அரச கᾞம ெமாழி" என்ᾠ இᾞ வாக்கியங்களில் குறிப்பிட ேவண்ᾌம்? ஏன் "சிங்களெமாழி, தமிழ்ெமாழி, ஆங்கிலெமாழி ஆகிய ᾙம்ெமாழிகᾦம் அரச கᾞம ெமாழிகள்" என ஒேர வாக்கியத்தில் உள்ளடக்கியிᾞக்கக்கூடாᾐ? எனக் ேகட்க விᾞம்ᾗகின்ேறன். அவ்வாᾠ ெசய்திᾞக்க ᾙᾊᾜம்; ஆனால் ெசய்யவில்ைல. கடந்த காலங்களில் இந்த நாட்ᾊல் நைடᾙைறயில் இᾞந்ᾐவந்த அரசியலைமப்ᾗகள் ᾚலᾙம், அதிᾤம் விேசடமாக, 1978ஆம் ஆண்ᾊல் ெகாண்ᾌவரப்பட்ட தற்ேபாைதய அரசியலைமப்ᾗத் திᾞத்தங்களிᾕடாகᾫம் இன்ᾠ இந்த நாᾌ பல்ேவᾠ பிரச்சிைன கைளᾜம் பல்ேவᾠ சவால்கைளᾜம் எதிர்ெகாண்ᾊᾞக்கின்றᾐ. நாங்கள் ஏன் இந்தப் பிரச்சிைனகைளச் சாிவர இனங்கண்ᾌ ெகாள்வைத ஒᾞ சவாலாகக்ெகாண்ᾌ இவற்ைற மாற்றியைமக்க ᾙன்வரக்கூடாᾐ? நாங்கள் சமஷ்ᾊையப் பற்றிப் ேபசுவதற்கு ᾙன்னர் அல்லᾐ federation அல்லᾐ federal அல்லᾐ confederation ஐப் பற்றிப் ேபசுவதற்கு ᾙன்னர், இப்ேபாதிᾞக்கின்ற இந்த ஒற்ைறயாட்சி அரசியலைமப்பிᾤள்ள சரத்ᾐக்கள் சாியாக ᾓற்ᾠக்கு ᾓᾠᾪதம் நைடᾙைறப்பᾌத்தப்பட்ᾊᾞக்கின்றனவா என்பைதத் ேதᾊப் பார்க்கின்றெபாᾨᾐ, "இல்ைல" என்ேற கூறேவண்ᾌம். மக்கள் விᾌதைல ᾙன்னணியினராகிய நாங்கள் இதைன மிகத் ெதளிவாகக் கூᾠகின்ேறாம். விேசடமாக இந்த அரசியலைமப்ᾗச் சட்டத்தில் குறிப்பிட்ᾌள்ளவாᾠ தமிழ் மக்கᾦக்கான உாிைமகள் வழங்கப்பட்ᾊᾞக்கின்றதா என்பைதத் ேதᾊப்பார்க்கின்றெபாᾨᾐ, "இல்ைல" என்ற கᾞத்ேத இன்ᾠ

651 652

2008 ජුනි 19

ேமேலாங்கி நிற்கின்றᾐ. இத்தைகய கᾞத்ᾐக்கள் இᾞப்பதனால் விேசடமாக இலங்ைகக்கு எதிராகச் ெசயற்பᾌகின்ற நபர்கᾦக்கும் இலங்ைகக்கு எதிரான கᾞத்ᾐக்கைளக் ெகாண்ᾊᾞப்ேபாᾞக்கும் இைவ மிகᾫம் சாதகமாக இᾞக்கின்றன. அவர்கள், "இேதா! இலங்ைகயின் அரசியலைமப்ᾗச் சட்டத்ைதப் பாᾞங்கள்! இதிᾤம் தமிழ் மக்கள் ᾗறக்கணிக்கப்பட்ᾊᾞக்கின்றார்கள்" என்ᾠ குறிப்பிடக்கூᾊய நிைலைமேய காணப்பᾌகிறᾐ. அதனால்தான் விேசடமாக இத்தைகய கᾞத்ᾐக்கᾧடாக இன்ᾠ தமிழ் மக்கள் ᾗறக்கணிக்கப்பட்ᾊᾞக்கின்றெபாᾨᾐ இந்த அரசியலைமப்பின் பதிேனழாவᾐ திᾞத்தச் சட்டம் உட்பட இந்த அரசியலைமப்ᾗச் சட்டம் சாியான ᾙைறயில் நைடᾙைறப்பᾌத்தப்பᾌமானால், இன்ᾠ இலங்ைகக்கு ஏற்பட்ᾌள்ள அபகீர்த்தியிᾢᾞந்ᾐ, அந்த அபாக்கியமான சந்தர்ப்பத்திᾢᾞந்ᾐ நாங்கள் நிச்சயமாக மீளᾙᾊᾜம் என்ற நம்பிக்ைக எங்கᾦக்கு இᾞக்கிறᾐ என நாங்கள் கூᾠகின்ேறாம். ஆனால், இந்த நாட்ᾊல் ஆட்சிக்கு வந்ᾐள்ள அரசாங்கங்களின் நடவᾊக்ைககைளத் ேதᾊப் பார்க்கின்றெபாᾨᾐ - மிக மிக ேவதைனப்பட ேவண்ᾊய விடயம் - அந்த அரசாங்கம் பதவிக்கு - அரசாட்சிக்கு வᾞவதற்கு ᾙன்ᾗ, "நாங்கள் ஆட்சிபீடம் ஏறியᾫடன் நல்லாட்சிைய உᾞவாக்குவதற்காக இந்த நாட்ᾊன் அரசிலைமப்ᾗச் சட்டத்ைத மக்கᾦக்கு நன்ைம பயக்கக்கூᾊயதாக மாற்றி யைமப்ேபாம்" என்ᾠ கூᾠகின்றவர்கள், ஆட்சிபீடம் ஏறிய பின்னர், அவர்கள் ஆட்சிக்கு வᾞவதற்கு ᾙன்னர் கூறிய அைனத்ைதᾜம் ᾗறந்தள்ளிவிட்ᾌத் தங்களᾐ ᾗதிய நிகழ்ச்சிநிரைல ᾙன்ெனᾌப்பதற்காக இந்த அரசியலைமப்ᾗச் சட்டத்ைதச் சாிவர நைடᾙைறப்பᾌத்ᾐவதிᾢᾞந்ᾐ பின்னᾊக்கின்றைமேய நைட ெபற்ᾠ வந்திᾞக்கின்றᾐ. அதற்குச் சிறந்த உதாரணமாக, அண்ைமயில் கிழக்கு மாகாணத்தில் நைடெபற்ற ேதர்தைலக் குறிப்பிடலாம். கடந்த இᾞபᾐ வᾞட காலமாக கிழக்கு மாகாண மக்கள் ᾜத்தத்தினால் பீᾊக்கப்பட்ᾊᾞந்தார்கள். ெகளரவ பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கேள, கிழக்கு மாகாணத்தில் மட்ᾌம் நாற்பதாயிரத்ᾐக்கும் அதிகமான விதைவப் ெபண்கள் இᾞப்பதாகக் கூறப்பᾌகிறᾐ; இரண்ᾌ இலட்சத்ᾐக்கும் அதிகமான பிள்ைளகள் தாய் தந்ைதயைர இழந்த நிைலயில் அநாைதகளாக்கப் பட்ᾌ அகதிகளாக வாழ்வதாகக் கூறப்பᾌகிறᾐ. அைதவிட, மந்த ேபாசைணயாᾤம் ேபாஷாக்கு இன்றிᾜம் வாᾊ வதங்குகின்ற பிள்ைளகள் எங்கு இᾞக்கிறார்கள் என்பைதத் ேதᾊப் பார்க்கின்ற ெபாᾨᾐ, அவர்கᾦம் கிழக்கு மாகாணத்திேலேய இᾞக்கிறார்கள் எனத் ெதாியவᾞகிறᾐ. தமிழ் மக்கள் கூᾌதலாக வாழ்கின்ற பிரேதசங்களாகிய வட மாகாணத்ைதᾜம், கிழக்கு மாகாணத் திᾤள்ள மட்டக்களப்ᾗ, அம்பாைற மாவட்டங்கைளᾜம் எᾌத்ᾐப் பார்க்கின்றெபாᾨᾐ, அைவ மிகᾫம் பின்தங்கிய நிைலயிேலேய இᾞக்கின்றன. அப்பிரேதசங்கள் கடந்த இᾞபᾐ வᾞட காலமாக ᾜத்தத்தினால் பாதிக்கப்பட்ᾊᾞந்ததன் காரணமாகப் பின்தங்கிய நிைலயில் இᾞக்கின்றன. விேசடமாக, தமிழீழ விᾌதைலப் ᾗᾢகளின் ஆட்சியதிகாரம் நைடெபற்றதாகக் கூறப்பᾌகின்ற பிரேதசங்கைள நாங்கள் ேதᾊப் பார்க்கின்றெபாᾨᾐ, அங்குள்ள மக்கள்தான் மிகுந்த ேவதைனயிᾤம் ᾐன்பத்திᾤம் வாᾊக் ெகாண்ᾊᾞக்கின்றார்கள். அᾐதான் உண்ைம. இதைன அைனவᾞம் ஏற்ᾠக்ெகாள்வார்கள் என்ேற நிைனக்கின்ேறன். ஏெனனில் நான் அப்பிரேதசங்கᾦக்கு ெசன்ᾠ அங்குள்ள மக்களின் நிைலைமகைள ேநரᾊயாகப் பார்ைவயிட்டவன்; அந்த மக்கᾦடன் ேபசியவன் என்ற ᾙைறயில் அங்குள்ள இவ்வாறான நிைலைமகைளக் குறிப்பிᾌகின்ேறன்.

அப்பᾊயானால் அந்த மக்கள் எைத எதிர்பார்த்தார்கள்? தாங்கள் இந்த ெநᾞக்கᾊயிᾢᾞந்ᾐ மீளேவண்ᾌம் ; தங்கᾦக்குப் பலவந்த மாகத் திணிக்கப்பட்ᾊᾞக்கின்ற கᾞத்ᾐக்கைள ஒᾐக்கிவிட்ᾌ தாங்கள் சுதந்திரமாகச் சிந்திக்கேவண்ᾌம் ; தாங்கள் சுதந்திரமாக ᾙᾊெவᾌக்கேவண்ᾌம் என்ᾠ எண்ணிக்ெகாண்ᾊᾞந்த ேவைளயில் தான் அங்கு உள்ᾧராட்சிச் சைபத் ேதர்தல்கள் நைடெபற்றன. அந்தத் ேதர்தல் நைடெபᾠம்ேபாᾐ மக்கள் விᾌதைல ᾙன்னணிையச் ேசர்ந்த நாங்கள் கூறிேனாம், "இந்தத் ேதர்தᾢல்

நாங்கள் கலந்ᾐெகாள்ளப்ேபாவதில்ைல; ஆனால், அங்கு ேதர்தல் நடத்ᾐவதற்கான உாிைம இᾞக்கிறᾐ. அங்கிᾞக்கின்ற மக்கᾦக்கு ஜனநாயக உாிைமகள் ெபற்ᾠக்ெகாᾌக்கப்படேவண்ᾌம். அந்தக் கிராமங்களில் வாᾊக்ெகாண்ᾊᾞக்கின்ற மக்களᾐ பிரச்சிைன கைளத் தீர்ப்பதற்கு கீழ்மட்டத்தில் இᾞக்கின்ற அைனத்ᾐ உள்ᾧராட்சி நிᾠவனங்கᾦம் நல்ல ᾙைறயில் நைடᾙைறப் பᾌத்தப்பட ேவண்ᾌம்; அதᾕடாக அந்தப் பிரேதசத்தில் இᾞக்கின்ற பிரச்சிைனகைள இனங்கண்ᾌ தீர்ப்பதற்கு ஏᾐவான நடவᾊக்ைககள் எᾌக்கப்படேவண்ᾌம்" என்ᾠ. அந்த உள்ᾧராட்சிச் சைபத் ேதர்தᾢல் அரசாங்கம் அல்லᾐ அரசாங்கம் சார்பான அரசியல் கட்சிகள் அல்லᾐ இயக்கங்கள் ெவற்றிெபற்றன என்பᾐ அைனவᾞக்கும் நன்றாகத் ெதாிᾜம். ெகளரவ பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கேள, அவர்கள் ெவற்றி ெபற்ற அᾌத்த நிமிடேம என்ன ெசய்திᾞக்க ேவண்ᾌம்? இந்த அரசியலைமப்பில் இᾞக்கின்ற சரத்ᾐகைளச் சாியான ᾙைறயில் நைடᾙைறப்பᾌத்தி யிᾞக்கேவண்ᾌம். ஆனால், 'கிழக்கின் உதயம்' என்ᾠ கூறப் பᾌகிறᾐ. உண்ைமயிேல கிழக்கில் உதயம் நிகழ்கிறதா அல்லᾐ கிழக்கு ெவᾦக்கின்றதா என்ᾠ நாங்கள் ேதᾊப்பார்க்கின்றேபாᾐ இன்னᾙம் கிழக்கு இᾞளாகேவ இᾞப்பᾐ ெதாிகிறᾐ.

கிழக்கு மாகாண சைபத் ேதர்தᾢன்ேபாᾐ நாங்கள் அங்கு ெசன்றிᾞந்ேதாம். அேதேவைள, கிழக்கு மாகாணத்ᾐக்கு அைனத்ᾐ அைமச்சர்கᾦம் வந்திᾞந்தார்கள். கிழக்கில் இᾞபᾐ வᾞடங்களாக ᾜத்த பீதியில் வாழ்கின்ற மக்கைள அதிᾢᾞந்ᾐ மீட்ெடᾌத்ᾐ அவர்கள் சுதந்திரமாகச் சிந்தித்ᾐச் ெசயற்பᾌவதற்கான சந்தர்ப்பத்ைதப் ெபற்ᾠக்ெகாᾌப்பார்கள் என்ᾠ அங்குள்ள மக்கᾦம் எதிர்பார்த்தார்கள்; நிச்சயமாக நாங்கள்கூட எதிர்பார்த்ேதாம். ஆனால், ெகளரவ பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கேள, அᾐ நைடெபறாதᾐ மிகᾫம் ேவதைனக்குாிய விடயமாகும். மாகாண சைபைய உᾞவாக்கித்தᾞம்பᾊ அந்த மக்கள் ேகட்கவில்ைல. அவர்கள், தங்களᾐ பிரேதசத்ைதக் கட்ᾊெயᾨப்ᾗ மாᾠம் தாங்கள் சுயமாகச் சிந்திப்பதற்கான சூழைல ஏற்பᾌத்ᾐமாᾠம் அங்கிᾞக்கின்ற ஆᾜதக் குᾨக்களிடமிᾞந்ᾐ தங்கைள மீட்ெடᾌக்குமாᾠம் தாங்கள் சுதந்திரமாகச் சிந்தித்ᾐச் ெசயற்பᾌவதற்கான சந்தர்ப்பத்ைதப் ெபற்ᾠத்தᾞமாᾠம்தான் ேகட்டார்கள். அவ்வாᾠ கூறிᾜம் மாகாணசைப அவர்கள்மீᾐ திணிக்கப்பட்டᾐ. அந்த மாகாண சைபயிᾕடாக இன்ᾠ அரசியல் நிகழ்ᾫகள் ேவᾠ விதமாக மாற்றப்பட்ᾊᾞக்கின்றன. அவ்வாᾠ மாற்றப்பட்டாᾤம், அந்த மக்கள் இன்னᾙம் அேத ᾐன்பக் ேகணியில் தத்தளித்ᾐக் ெகாண்ᾊᾞக்கிறார்கள். அவ்வாᾠ தத்தளித்ᾐக் ெகாண்ᾊᾞக்கும்ேபாᾐ மᾠᾗறத்தில் ஏைனய நாᾌகள் அல்லᾐ ஏகாதிபத்திய சக்திகள் அல்லᾐ எமᾐ அண்ைட நாᾌகள் என்பவற்றின் நிகழ்ச்சி நிரல் எம்மீᾐ திணிக்கப்பட்ᾊᾞக்கிறᾐ. அதனால் இன்ᾠ கிழக்கு ெவᾦக்கவில்ைல; கிழக்கு மாகாண மக்கள் நிம்மதியாக வாழவில்ைல; ெதாடர்ந்ᾐம் ேவதைனᾜடன் வாழ்ந்ᾐ வᾞகிறார்கள். அதனால் ெகளரவ பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கேள, மக்கள் விᾌதைல ᾙன்னணிையச் ேசர்ந்த நாங்கள் கூᾠகின்ேறாம், கிழக்கில் வாழ்கின்ற தமிழ் மக்களினᾐ மட்ᾌமல்ல, வடக்கு - கிழக்கில் வாழ்கின்ற தமிழ் மக்களᾐ நம்பிக்ைகைய ெவன்ெறᾌக்கேவண்ᾌெமன்றால், நிச்சயமாக அரசியலைமப்பின் பதிேனழாவᾐ திᾞத்தச் சட்டம் சாியான ᾙைறயில் நைடᾙைறப்பᾌத்தப்படேவண்ᾌம் என்ᾠ. அதைன நைடᾙைறப்பᾌத்ᾐவதᾕடாகத்தான் அந்த மக்கᾦக்கு அரசாங் கத்தின்மீᾐ அல்லᾐ இந்த அரசியலைமப்பின்மீᾐ இᾞக்கின்ற அவநம்பிக்ைகையப் ேபாக்கᾙᾊᾜம். ஆகேவ, உடனᾊயாக இந்தப் பதிேனழாவᾐ திᾞத்தச் சட்டத்ைத நைடᾙைறப்பᾌத்ᾐவதற்கு நடவᾊக்ைக எᾌங்கள் என்ᾠ கூறிக்ெகாண்ᾌ, எனᾐ உைரைய ᾙᾊத்ᾐக்ெகாள்கிேறன். நன்றி.

නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමා (பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கள்) (The Deputy Speaker) ෙබොෙහොම ස්තුතියි. මී ළඟට, ගරු ඩිව් ගුණෙසේකර අමාතɕතුමා.

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව

[අ.භා. 5.02] ගරු ඩිව් ගුණෙසේකර මහතා (ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථා හා ජාතික ඒකාබද්ධතා අමාතɕතුමා)

(மாண்ᾗமிகு ᾊᾝ குணேசகர - அரசியலைமப்ᾗ அᾤவல்கள், ேதசிய ஒᾞைமப்பாட்ᾌ அைமச்சர்) (The Hon. Dew Gunasekara -Minister of Constitutional Affairs and National Integration) ගරු නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමනි, විපක්ෂෙය් පධාන සංවිධායකතුමා විසින් ඉදිරිපත් කරනු ලැබූ ෙමම ෙයෝජනා සවස 5.30 වන තුරු විවාද කරන්න අවස්ථාව ෙදන්නය කියා එතුමා ඉල්ලා සිටියා. ඒත් දැන් එතුමාත් ෙම් ගරු සභාෙව් නැහැ. මම හිතන විධියට ෙම් සම්බන්ධෙයන් සිදු වුණු ෙද් පිළිබඳව සැබෑ ෙතොරතුරු දන්න එක් ෙකනා එතුමායි. ඒ නිසා ෙම් සම්බන්ධෙයන් කරුණු ඉදිරිපත් කිරීෙම් දී මුහුණ ෙදන්න බැරි නිසා ද ෙකොෙහද එතුමා දැන් ෙම් ගරු සභාෙව් ඇත්ෙත් නැහැ. ගරු නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමනි, මෙග් කථාවට මා වැඩි ෙව්ලාවක් ගන්ෙන් නැහැ. මෙග් සෙහෝදර ගරු අමාතɕතුමන් ෙම් සම්බන්ධව විස්තරාත්මකව කරුණු ඉදිරිපත් කළා. ඒත් ෙම් මුළු විවාදය ගත්තාම පැය පහ හමාරක් යන තුරු කළ සියලු කථා මා අහෙගන හිටියා. නමුත් ෙම් විෂයට අදාළ කථා ඉදිරිපත් වුෙණ් ටිකයි. විෙශේෂෙයන් බාහිර ෙද්වල් තමයි වැඩි පුර කථා වුෙණ්. එය සම්පදායානුකූලව, හැම දාම අෙප් ෙම් සභා ගර්භෙය් සිදු වන ෙදයක්. ගරු නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමනි, ෙමොනවා වුණත් ෙම් පිළිබඳව විවාදයක් කරන්න අවස්ථාවක් ලබා දීම ගැන මා විපක්ෂයට ස්තුතිවන්ත ෙවනවා. මන්ද, ජනමාධɕ ෙතොරෙතෝංචියක් නැතිව දිගින් දිගටම ෙම් පශ්නය මතු කරමින් විශාල වɕාපාරයක් ෙගන යනවා. දැන් එය ජාතɕන්තර ක්ෙෂේතයටත් ගිහින්. එම නිසා ෙම් පිළිබඳව සැබෑ තත්ත්වය මහ ජනතාවට දැනුම් දීමට අවස්ථාවක් ලබා දීම ගැන මා සන්ෙතෝෂ ෙවනවා. ඇත්ත වශෙයන්ම මා කරුණු ඉදිරිපත් කරන්ෙන්, දහහත්වන ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථා සංෙශෝධනය කියාත්මක කිරීම විමර්ශනය කිරීම සඳහා වන විෙශේෂ කාරක සභාෙව් සභාපතිවරයා වශෙයන් ෙනොෙවයි; ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථා හා ජාතික ඒකාබද්ධතා ඇමතිවරයා වශෙයනුයි. ෙමොකද, දහහත්වන ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථා සංෙශෝධනය කියාත්මක කිරීම විමර්ශනය කිරීම සඳහා වන විෙශේෂ කාරක සභාව පිළිබඳව එක වචනයක්වත්, ඒ පිළිබඳව කරුණු කිසි ෙදයක්වත් මතු කරනු ලැබුෙව් නැහැ. මා ඒ ගැන නිගමනය කරන්ෙන්, දහහත්වන ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථා සංෙශෝධනය කියාත්මක කිරීම විමර්ශනය කිරීම සඳහා වන විෙශේෂ කාරක සභාව ෙකෙරහි විශ්වාසයක් ගරු මන්තීතුමන්ලාට තිෙබනවාය කියන එකයි. ඒ පිළිබඳව කිසිදු විෙව්චනයක් ෙකරිලා නැහැ. ඇත්ත වශෙයන්ම අෙප් ඉහත විෙශේෂ කාරක සභාෙව් අන්තර් වාර්තාව ගැන සාකච්ඡා කරන්න දින දමා ෙගන ති බුෙණ් අදටයි. ෙම් විවාදය නිසා මට ඒකත් කල් දමන්න සිදු වුණා. ගරු නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමනි, ඇත්ත වශෙයන්ම ෙමතැනදී ෙමොකක්ද සිදු වුෙණ්? පළමු වැනි ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථා සභාව පිහිටු වනු ලැබුෙව් 2002 මාර්තු මාසෙය් 22 වැනි දායි. අවුරුදු තුනක් ඉකුත් වන විට 2005 මාර්තු මස 21 වැනි දාට එය අෙහෝසි වුණා. අෙහෝසි වුණායින් පසුව, ෙද වැනි ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථා සභාව පත් කරන්න අවශɕයි. එහිදී ඒ අවශɕතාව පැන නැඟුණා. ඒ අනුව ඒ කියාදාමය ඉදිරියට ගියා. අතිගරු ජනාධිපතිතුමා පත් කළා, තමන්ෙග් නිෙයෝජිතයා. ගරු අගමැතිතුමා පත් කළා, තමන්ෙග් නිෙයෝජිතයා. ගරු විපක්ෂ නායකතුමා පත් කළා, තමන්ෙග් නිෙයෝජිතයා. ඒ ආකාරෙයන් ඉදිරියට ගියා. එෙහත් ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථාෙව් දහහත්වන සංෙශෝධනය යටෙත් ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථා සභාවක් ස්ථාපිත වීමට ඒ සාමාජිකයන් දහ ෙදනාෙගන්ම එය සමන්විත විය යුතුයි. ෙම්ක තමයි පැහැදිලිව නීතිපතිවරයා දී තිෙබන අර්ථ කථනය. නමුත්, ඒ අවස්ථාව වන විට සාමාජිකයන් නව ෙදනකු පමණයි සිටිෙය්. දහ වැනි සාමාජිකයා ෙතෝරා ගැනීෙම් අර්බුදයක් පැන නැඟුණා. ඒ අර්බුදය ආණ්ඩුෙව් අර්බුදයක් ෙනොෙවයි. ඒක අතිගරු

ජනාධිපතිතුමාෙග් අර්බුදයක් ෙනොෙවයි. ඒක ගරු කථානායකතුමාෙග් පැත්ෙතන් වුණු අර්බුදයක් ෙනොෙවයි. එය විපක්ෂය පැත්ෙතන් වුණු අර්බුදයක්. ෙමතැනදී ඒ පශ්නය මතු වුෙණ් නැහැ. දහ වැනි සාමාජිකයා ෙතෝරා ගත යුත්ෙත් සුළුතර පක්ෂවලිනුයි. එතැන තිබුණු පශ්නය ෙමොකක් ද? ජාතික ෙහළ උරුමය, - JHU එක - TNA එක, Sri Lanka Muslim Congress එක කියන ෙම් පක්ෂ තුනට තමන්ෙග් නිෙයෝජිතයා ෙතෝරා ගැනීෙම් ෙපොදු එකඟත්වයකට එන්න බැරි වීමයි. 2005 අවුරුද්ෙද් සිට 2007 අවුරුද්ෙද් ෙපබරවාරි මාසය දක්වා අවුරුදු ෙදකක් වන තුරු එකඟත්වයකට එන්න බැරි වුණා. ඉතින් කාෙග්ද වරද? වරද අතිගරු ජනාධිපතිතුමාෙග් ද? වරද ගරු කථානායකතුමාෙග්ද? වරද ගරු අගමැතිතුමාෙග් ද? වරද අමාතɕවරයා වශෙයන් මෙග්ද? නැහැ, වරද විපක්ෂෙය්යි. විපක්ෂෙයනුත් සමස්ත විපක්ෂෙය් ෙනොෙවයි. TNA එක, JHU එක, Sri Lanka Muslim Congress එක කියන පක්ෂවලටයි ෙපොදු consensus එකකට එන්න බැරි වුෙණ්. ඒකට අප ෙදොස් කියන්ෙන් නැහැ. එවැනි තත්ත්වයක් මතු ෙවන්න පුළුවන්. නමුත්, ඇත්ත වශෙයන්ම සිදු වුෙණ් ඒකයි. මා දන්නවා ගරු කථානායකතුමාත් ෙම් පක්ෂ එක්ක සාකච්ඡා කර, කිහිප වතාවක්ම උත්සාහ ගත්තා ෙම් තුන් ෙගොල්ලන්ටම පිළිගත හැකි වන පරිදි ෙම් සඳහා ෙකනකු ෙයෝජනා කරන්න. ඒ කියන්ෙන් තමන්ෙග් පක්ෂවලින් ෙනොෙවයි, සමාජයට පිළිගත හැකි පුද්ගලයකු ෙයෝජනා කරන්නයි. ඒත් අවුරුදු ෙදකක් යන තුරු බැරි වුණා. දැන් ඒ අවස්ථාව වන විට ෙමොකක්ද රෙට් වɕවස්ථාව? ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථා සභාවක් නැහැ. ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථා සභාවක් නැති නිසා අතිගරු ජනාධිපතිතුමා ෙමොකක්ද, කළ යුත්ෙත්? අෙප් පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුවට කළ හැක්ෙක් ෙමොකක්ද? කිසිම ෙදයක් නැහැ. අධිකරණයට කළ හැක්ෙක් ෙමොකක්ද? කිසි ෙදයක් නැහැ. අධිකරණයටත් බැහැ, වɕවස්ථාදායකයටත් බැහැ, විධායකටත් බැහැ. අර්බුදකාරි තත්ත්වයක් තිෙබන්ෙන්. ෙමෙහම තමයි, දහහත්වන ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථා සංෙශෝධනය කඩිමුඩිෙය් සකස් කෙළේ. මා හිතන හැටියට මහින්ද සමරසිංහ ඇමතිතුමාත්, ඒ වාෙග්ම ලාල්කාන්ත මන්තීතුමාත් ෙම් පිළිබඳව පැහැදිලිව කරුණු ඉදිරිපත් කළා. මහ රෑ වන තුරු විවාද කරලා ෙම් ෙපොදු එකඟත්වයට ආෙව් හදිසිෙය්යි. හදිසියක් තිබුණා. කඩිමුඩියක් තිබුණා. වුවමනාවක් තිබුණා. ෙම්ක ඇත්ත වශෙයන්ම කියාත්මක වුෙණ් අර සංහිඳියා ආණ්ඩුව යටෙත්යි. ජනාධිපති වශෙයන් චන්දිකා කුමාරතුංග මැතිනිය එක පැත්තකිනුත්, අගමැති වශෙයන් රනිල් විකමසිංහ මහත්මයා අනික් පැත්ෙතනුත් සිටින වකවානුෙව් තමයි, ෙමය කියාත්මක ෙවන්න පටන් ගත්ෙත්. සමහර විට අගමැතිතුමාට ෙම්ෙක් වුවමනාකම තිබුණා. නමුත් පශ්නය තිෙබන්ෙන් කවුද, වග කිව යුත්ෙත්, වරද පැට විය හැක්ෙක් කාටද කියන එකයි. ඒක අවුරුදු ෙදකක්, තුනක් වන තුරුම ගියා. ඉතින් ඒ අවස්ථාව වන විට රෙට් නායකයා විධියට, රාජɕ නායකයා විධියට ජනාධිපතිතුමාට අහක බලා ෙගන ඉන්න පුළුවන්ද? Million එකක් පමණ රජෙය් ෙසේවකයන් ඉන්නවා. ඒ වන විට රාජɕ ෙසේවා ෙකොමිෂන් සභාව ඇතුළු අනිකුත් ෙකොමිෂන් සභා සියල්ෙල්ම නිල කාලය අවසන් වුණා. කිසිම ෙකොමිෂන් සභාවක් නැහැ, කියාත්මක ෙවන්න. රට තුළ අරාජික තත්ත්වයක් මතු ෙවන්න පටන් ගත්තා. ඒ අරාජික තත්ත්වයක් යටෙත් රාජɕ නායකයා නිකම් බලා ෙගන ඉන්නවාද, ෙම්ක මෙග් job එකක් ෙනොෙවයි, ෙම්ක පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුෙව් job එකක් කියලා. මා හිතන හැටියට එතුමා රාජɕ නායකයා විධියට එඩිතරව පියවරක් ගත්තා, ෙකොමිෂන් සභා පත් කරන්න. මෙග් මිත ගරු මන්තීතුමා කිව්වා, ෙම්ක ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථාව උල්ලංඝනය කිරීමක්ය කියලා. ෙවන්න පුළුවන්. ඒ අර්ථ කථනය ෙදන්න ඕනෑ, ෙශේෂ්ඨාධිකරණය විසිනුයි. අපි කාටවත් ෙශේෂ්ඨාධිකරණයට යන්න එපාය කිව්ෙව් නැහැ. 2005 සිට 2008 දක්වා අවුරුදු තුනක් තිස්ෙසේ ඕනෑම පුරවැසියකුට ෙශේෂ්ඨාධිකරණයට යන්න පුළුවන් ඉඩකඩක් තිබුණා. ඕනෑම පුරවැසියකුට ෙශේෂ්ඨාධිකරණයට ගිහින්, කරුණු ඉදිරිපත් කරලා, ජනාධිපතිතුමා ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථාව උල්ලංඝනය කළාය කියා තීන්දුවක් ගන්න තිබුණා. ඒ ඉඩකඩ අප අවහිර කෙළේ නැහැ. නමුත් ඇත්ත වශෙයන්ම මූලිකව ඒකට වග කියන්න ඕනෑ, ෙම් ගරු සභාවයි, ෙවන කවුරුවත් ෙනොෙවයි. ෙම් ගරු සභාව අසමර්ථ වුණා, ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථා සභාව නිසියාකාර

655 656

2008 ජුනි 19

ෙලස ස්ථාපිත කරන්න. ඒක පක්ෂ කීපයක පශ්නයක් වුණත් සමස්ත වශෙයන් වග කියන්න ඕනෑ පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුවයි. එෙහම නම් පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුෙව් අසාර්ථකත්වය පිළිගන්ෙන් නැතිව ෙම්ක ෙවන ෙකනකුට - ජනාධිපතිවරයාට, නැත්නම් අධිකරණයට ෙහෝ ෙවන කාටවත් - පටවන්න පුළුවන්කමක් නැහැ. එය තමන් අතින් වුණු වරදක්. එෙසේ නම් ඒ වරද සිදු වුෙණ් ඊට එහා ගිහින් තවත් තැනක. මූලික වශෙයන්ම ෙම් දහහත්වන ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථාව කියවා බැලුෙවොත් සුපිම් උසාවිය - ෙශේෂ්ඨාධිකරණය - ෙම්ක අනුමත කෙළේ ෙකොෙහොමද කියා මා දන්ෙන් නැහැ. ඕනෑම ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථාවක සංෙශෝධනයක් වන විට ඒක ෙශේෂ්ඨාධිකරණයට යනවා. ඒක හිතා ගන්නත් බැහැ, ආධුනිකයන් විසින් සකස් කරපු ෙදයක් විධියට තමයි ෙමය ෙපෙනන්ෙන්. ඒ තරමට දුර්වලකම්, අඩු ලුහුඬුකම් ෙගොඩක් තිෙබනවා. ඒ නිසා තමයි ෙම් අර්බුදය ආෙව්. මා නිදර්ශනයක් කියන්නම්. ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථා සභාවක් තිෙබන්න ඕනෑ අඛණ්ඩව ඉදිරියට යන්න. අවුරුදු තුන පැන්නාම අතර මඟ කඩා වැෙටන්න බැහැ. නමුත් ඒක හදා තිෙබන්ෙන් අතර මඟ කඩා වැෙටන්නමයි. දැන් අප ඒක සකස් කරලා සංෙශෝධන ෙග්නවා අඛණ්ඩව යන්න. පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව විසුරුවා හැ රියත් ඒක යන්න ඕනෑ. ෙකොමිෂන් සභා විසුරුවා හැරියත්, ඒ කාල පරිච්ෙඡ්දය අවසන් වුණත් ඒක දිගට යන්න ඕනෑ. පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව විසුරුවා හැරියත් ඒ සියල්ලම යන්න ඕනෑ. ඒක දැක්ෙක් නැහැ. දැක්මක් නැතිව තමයි දහහත්වන ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථා සංෙශෝධනය හදලා තිෙබන්ෙන්. හදිසිෙය්, කඩිමු ඩිෙය් කිසිම දැක්මක් නැතිව, ගැඹුරට අධɕයනය කරන්ෙන් නැතිවයි එය හදා තිෙබන්ෙන්. අවුරුදු කීපයකින් ෙම්ක ඉස්සරහට යන විට විෙශේ ෂෙයන් අප වාෙග් සමාජයක ෙද්ශපාලන වශෙයන් සංකීර්ණ තත්ත්වයක් තිෙබන අවස්ථාවක - ගරු දිමුතු බණ්ඩාර අබයෙකෝන් මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு திᾙத்ᾐ பண்டார அபயேகான்) (The Hon. Dimuthu Bandara Abayakoon) ඔබතුමාත් එතෙකොට හිටියා. ගරු ඩිව් ගුණෙසේකර මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ᾊᾝ குணேசகர) ( The Hon. Dew Gunasekara) ඇත්ත වශෙයන් මා ඡන්දය දුන්ෙන් නැහැ. මා එතෙකොට හිටිෙය් නැහැ. ෙපෞද්ගලිකව ෙනොෙවයි ෙම් පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුෙවන් ඡන්දය ගත්ෙත්. ඒ කාලෙය් ඔබතුමා හිටියා නම් වග කියන්න ඕනෑ. මා නම් හිටිෙය් නැහැ. ගරු දිමුතු බණ්ඩාර අබයෙකෝන් මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு திᾙத்ᾐ பண்டார அபயேகான்) (The Hon. Dimuthu Bandara Abayakoon) ඒ කාලෙය් ජනාධිපතිතුමා හිටියා ෙන්. ගරු ඩිව් ගුණෙසේකර මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ᾊᾝ குணேசகர) ( The Hon. Dew Gunasekara) ජනාධිපතිතුමා ෙනොෙවයි. මම කියන්ෙන් ෙම් පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව කරපු ෙදයක්. ෙම්ක ෙගනාෙව් තමුන්නාන්ෙසේලා. එක්සත් ජාතික පක්ෂය තමයි ෙම්ක ආරම්භ කෙළේ. ඒ නිසා ඒ ගැන තර්ක කරන්න යන්න එපා. ඒ වරද අපි කවුරුත් පිළිගනිමු. [බාධා කිරීමක්] පනත ෙමතැනින් ෙන් සකස් කෙළේ. ඔබතුමා ලාල්කාන්ත මන්තීතුමාෙග් කථාව අහ ෙගන හිටියා ෙන් ෙකොෙහොමද ෙකරුෙණ් කියලා. තවත් අහන්න වැඩක් නැහැ ෙන්? කරුණාකර මෙග් කාලය නාස්ති කරන්න එපා. ගරු නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමනි, ඊට පස්ෙසේ තත්ත්වය තවත් වɕාකූල වුණා. ෙමොකද, ජනතා විමුක්ති ෙපරමුණ ආණ්ඩුව පැත්ෙත් ඉඳලා අනික් පැත්තට ගියා. අනික් පැත්තට ගිහින් කිව්වා, "සුළුතරෙය් නිෙයෝජිතයා ෙත්රීෙම් අයිතිය තිෙබන්ෙන් අපටයි, ටීඑන්ඒ එකට ෙනොෙවයි, ෙජ්එච්යූ එකට ෙනොෙවයි, මුස්ලිම් ෙකොංගසයට ෙනොෙවයි අපට තමයි වැඩි මන්තීවරු ගණනක් ඉන්ෙන්" කියා. දැන් තවත් අර්බුදයක්. [බාධා කිරීමක්]

ෙබ්රුෙව් 2007 ෙපබරවාරි මාසෙය්දී. මා එතැනට එන්නම්. ඉන්න. ෙම්ක තමයි පධානම ෙහේතුව. පමාද වුණු ෙහේතුව කවුරුවත් රටට කියන්ෙන් නැහැ. ෙම්ක තමයි සැබෑ ෙහේතුව. එදා ඒකට එකඟත්වයක් ආවා නම් අද ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථා සභාවත් තිෙබනවා, ෙකොමිෂන් සභාත් තිෙබනවා. ෙම් පශ්නය අද ෙමතැන සාකච්ඡා කරන්න අවශɕතාවක් මතු වන්ෙන්ත් නැහැ. ගරු ආර්. එම්. ගාමිණී රත්නායක මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ஆர். எம். காமினி ரத்நாயக்க) (The Hon. R. M. Gamini Rathnayake) ඇමතිතුමා, 2008?

ගරු ඩිව් ගුණෙසේකර මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ᾊᾝ குணேசகர) ( The Hon. Dew Gunasekara) 2008 තමයි. ෙමොකක්ද වුෙණ් කියා කියන්න ෙපොඩ්ඩක් අහ ෙගන ඉන්න.

ඊ ළඟට පක්ෂ නායකවරු ෙම් පශ්නය සාකච්ඡා කළා. ෙම් අර්බුදය ෙත්රුම් ගත්තා. ඊ ළඟට තමයි 2006 ජුලි මාසෙය් ෙම් සඳහා විෙශේෂ කාරක සභාවක් පත් කෙළේ. විෙශේෂ කාරක සභාව කියාත්මක වුණා. ඒ අතරතුර ෙම් සභා ගර්භය තුළ ෙද්ශපාලන වර්තනයන් ෙදකක් ඇති වුණා. ඊ ළඟට එක්සත් ජාතික පක්ෂය තීරණයක් ගත්තා විෙශේෂ කාරක සභාව වර්ජනය කරන්න. ෙහේතුව, කරු ජයසූරිය ඇමතිතුමා හා එක්සත් ජාතික පක්ෂෙයන් ආණ්ඩුව පැත්තට ගිය තවත් අය ඒ විෙශේෂ කාරක සභාෙව් ඉන්න තුරු අප එන්ෙන් නැහැය කීම. එවිට ගරු කථානායකතුමා කිව්වා, "මට ඒක කරන්න බැහැ, මට අයින් කරන්න බැහැ, ඔවුන් මන්තීවරු" කියා. ඇමතිවරයා විධියට, සභාපතිවරයා විධියට මා උත්සාහයක් ගත්තා අඩු ගණෙන් ඒ ෙදන්ෙනක් එහාට ගියා නම් තව අතිෙර්ක ෙදන්ෙනක් එක්සත් ජාතික පක්ෂයට දීලා ෙම් විෙශේෂ කාරක සභාව අප ඉස්සරහට අර ෙගන යමුය කියා. ඒක compromise එකක්. ඒක පිළිගත්ෙතත් නැහැ. දැන් වැඩ ඇන හිටලා. දැන් විපක්ෂ නායකතුමා ෙම් ගරු සභාෙව් හිටියා නම් මා කියනවා. මා හතර පාරක් විපක්ෂ නායකතුමා හම්බ ෙවලා ෙපෞද්ගලිකව කිව්වා, කරුණාකර ෙම් දහහත්වන ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථා සංෙශෝධනය ඉක්මන් කරන්න තමන්ෙග් නිෙයෝජිතයන්ට එන්න කියන්නය කියා. එෙහම කියලා තමයි අවසාන රැස්වීමට ෙචොක්සි මහත්මයා එව්ෙව්. මම ෙගෞරවෙයන් මතක් කරන්නට ඕනෑ, එතුමා ඇවිත් සංෙශෝධන ගණනාවක් ඉදිරිපත් කළ බව. ඒ සංෙශෝධන සියල්ලම වාෙග් අපි පිළිගත්තා. ඒ පිළිගත්ත සංෙශෝධන ඇතුළත් කරලා, අන්තර් වාර්තාව හදලා අද අපි රැස් වන්නයි හිටිෙය්. ඒ අතරතුර මට ආරංචියක් ලැබුණා, නැවත වරක් සභාව වර්ජනය කරන්න තීරණයක් අරෙගන තිෙබනවාය කියා. ෙචොක්සි මහත්මයාට යන්න එපාය කියා තිෙබනවාය කියා දැන ගන්නට ලැබුණා. එතුමා හිටියා නම් පිළිතුරක් ලබා ගන්න තිබුණා. සභාව වර්ජනය කිරීෙම් අදහසක් ඔවුන් තුළ තිෙබන්න ෙහේතුව ෙමොකක්ද? ෙම් අර්බුදය ඉස්සරහට අරෙගන යෑමයි. අර්බුදය ඉස්සරහට අරෙගන යන්නද වුවමනාව තිෙබන්ෙන්? විපක්ෂ නායකතුමාට අවශɕ, ෙම් අර්බුදය ඉස්සරහට අරෙගන ගිහින්, "ෙමන්න ජනාධිපතිතුමා ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථාව අමු අමුෙව් උල්ලංඝනය කරනවා" කියන සටන් පාඨය ඔස්ෙසේ ෙම් රට තුළයි, ජාතɕන්තර වශෙයනුයි campaign එකක් අරන් යන්නද? ඒ නිසා මා විපක්ෂෙයන් ඉල්ලා සිටිනවා, විෙශේෂෙයන් එක්සත් ජාතික පක්ෂෙයන් මා ඉල්ලා සිටිනවා, කරුණාකර ඊ ළඟ රැස්වීමට ෙචොක්සි මහත්තයාට එන්න කියන්නය කියලා. සියල්ල අවසාන කරන තත්ත්වයකටයි අපි ඇවිත් තිෙබන්ෙන්. අපි එක්කාසු ෙවලා ෙම්වා සියල්ල අනුමත කළාම මට පුළුවන් ෙවනවා, පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුවට අන්තර් වාර්තාව ඉදිරිපත් කරන්න. එතෙකොට ඇමති මණ්ඩලයට අවස්ථාවක් ලැෙබනවා, එය ෙකටුම්පත් කරන්න. ඒ ෙකටුම්පත අරෙගන අපට ෙමතැනට එන්න පුළුවන්. ෙමෙහම තමයි අර්බුදය විසඳන්න ෙවන්ෙන්. නැතුව ෙවනත් මාර්ගයක් ඇත්ෙත් නැහැ.

657 658

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව

[ගරු ඩිව් ගුණෙසේකර මහතා] ]

ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථා සභාවක් පත් ෙනොකර, ෙකොමිෂන් සභාත් පත් ෙනොකර එදා ජනාධිපතිතුමා නිහඬව සිටියා නම්, අවුරුදු ෙදකක් තුනක් යන ෙතක් නිහඬව සිටියා නම්, රජෙය් ෙසේවකයන්ෙග් දුක් ගැනවිලි, මාරු වීම්, පත්කිරීම් ෙම් සියල්ලක්ම ඇනහිටිනවා. එෙහම නම් ෙපොලිස් ෙකොමිෂන් එකකුත් නැහැ. එවැනි තත්ත්වයකදී ඇති වන අර්බුද වළක්වන්න තමයි ජනාධිපතිතුමාට රාජɕ නායකයා විධියට ෙම්කට මැදිහත් ෙවන්න සිද්ධ වුෙණ්. ජනාධිපතිතුමා ෙම් පත්වීම් සිදු කරන අවස්ථාව වන ෙතක්, 2005 සිට 2007 දක්වා විපක්ෂෙයන් ෙහෝ රට තුළ ෙහෝ කිසිම උද්ෙඝෝෂණයක් ෙම් ගැන මතු කෙළේ නැහැ. ඔවුන් නිහඬව සිටියා. නිහඬව සිටිෙය් තිබුණු යථාර්ථය ඔවුන් පිළිගත්ත නිසයි. ගරු නි ෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමනි, මා කියා සිටියා, ෙම් කාරක සභාෙව් වැඩ කටයුතු පමාද වීමට ෙහේතුව කුමක්ද කියා. ෙමහිදී විෙශේෂෙයන්ම සඳහන් කරන්න ඕනෑ කාරණා ෙදකක් තිෙබනවා. අවසානෙය් දහවන සාමාජිකයා පත් කරන්න තිබියදී මා කියා සිටියා, ජනාධිපතිතුමා ෙම්කට මැදිහත් ෙවන්න කටයුතු කරයි කියලා. ෙම් තත්ත්වයන් යටෙත් මා විෙශේෂෙයන්ම විපක්ෂයට කියා සිටින්ෙන් ෙම් පිළිබඳව දිගින් දිගටම රට තුළ ආ න්ෙදෝලනයක් ඇති කිරීමට අවශɕ ෙනොවන බවයි. තමන්ෙග් නි ෙයෝජිතයාටත් ෙම්කට සහභාගි ෙවන්න කියා කිව්ෙවොත් අපට වැඩි දවසක් ෙනොගිහින් ෙම් සංෙශෝධන ටික ෙගනැත් පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුවට අන්තර් වාර්තාව ඉදිරිපත් කරන්න පුළුවන්. එතෙකොට ඇමති මණ්ඩලයට අවස්ථාවක් ලැෙබනවා; ඉඩකඩ ලැෙබනවා, ඒ අන්තර් වාර්තාව ඇමති මණ්ඩලය තුළ සාකච්ඡා කරලා, ෙකටුම්පත් කරලා, දහහත්වන ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථා සංෙශෝධනයට අවශɕ සංෙශෝධන ඉදිරිපත් කරන්න.

ගරු නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමනි, ෙම් දහහත්වන ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථා සංෙශෝධනෙය් මුළුමනින්ම ෙවනස් කරන්න සිද්ධ වුණු කරුණු පහෙළොවක් විස්සක් විතර තිෙබන බවට අප දැනටමත් හඳුනා ෙගන තිෙබනවා. චන්දිකා බණ්ඩාරනායක කුමාරතුංග මැතිනිය ජනාධිපති වශෙයන් සිටි ෙව්ලාෙව් මැතිවරණ ෙකොමිෂන් සභාෙව් සභාපතිවරයා පත් කිරීම සම්බන්ධෙයන් එතුමිය එකඟ වුෙණ් නැහැ. එෙහම එකඟ ෙනොෙවනවා නම් ඊ ළඟට කළ යුතු ෙද් ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථාෙව් තිෙබන්න ඕනෑ. කළ යුත්ෙත් කුමක්ද? තවත් නමක් ඉල්ලා සිටිනවාද? එෙහම එකක් නැහැ. ෙම් දහහත්වන ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථාව හදලා තිෙයන්ෙන්ම අර්බුදෙයන් අර්බුදයට රට තල්ලු කරන්නයි. එෙහම එක් ෙදයක් පිළිගන්ෙන් නැත්නම් ඊ ළඟ අවස්ථාවක් තිෙබන්න ඕනෑ. ඒකට අවශɕ සංෙශෝධන දැන් අපි සකස් කර ෙගන තිෙබනවා. මා මීට වඩා කථා කරන්න බලාෙපොෙරොත්තු ෙවන්ෙන් නැහැ. ඒ නිසා ෙම් කාරණෙය්දී සාධනීය වශෙයන් වග කීෙමන් යුතුව කටයුතු කරන ෙලස විපක්ෂෙයන් ඉල්ලා සිටිමින් මා නිහඬ ෙවනවා. ෙබොෙහොම ස්තුතියි. පශ්නය විමසන ලදින්, සභා සම්මත විය. வினா விᾌக்கப்பட்ᾌ ஏற்ᾠsக்ெகாள்ளப்பட்டᾐ. Question put, and agreed to.

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව ඊට අනුකූලව අ. භා. 5.20 ට, 2008 ජූනි 20 වන සිකුරාදා පු.භා. 9.30 වන ෙතක් කල් ගිෙය්ය.

அதன்பᾊ பி. ப. 5.20 மணிக்கு பாராᾦமன்றம், 2008 ᾝன் 20, ெவள்ளிக்கிழைம ᾙ.ப. 9.30 மணிவைர ஒத்திைவக்கப்பட்டᾐ. Adjourned accordingly at 5.20 p.m. until 9.30 a.m. on Friday, 20th June, 2008.

659 660

குறிப்ᾗ

உᾠப்பினர் இᾠதிப் பதிப்பிற் ெசய்யவிᾞம்ᾗம் பிைழ திᾞத்தங்கைளத் தமᾐ பிரதியில் ெதளிவாகக் குறித்ᾐ அதைனப் பிைழ

திᾞத்தப்படாத பிரதி கிைடத்த இᾞ வாரங்கᾦள் ஹன்சாட் பதிப்பாசிாியᾞக்கு அᾔப்ᾗதல் ேவண்ᾌம்.

සැ.යු. ෙමම වාර්තාෙව් අවසාන මුදණය සදහා ස්වකීය නිවැරදි කළ යුතු තැන් දක්වනු රිසි මන්තීන් මින් පිටපතක් ෙගන නිවැරදි කළ යුතු ආකාරය එහි පැහැදිලිව ලකුණු ෙකොට, පිටපත ලැබී ෙදසතියක් ෙනොඉක්මවා හැන්සාඩ් සංස්කාරක ෙවත ලැෙබන ෙසේ එවිය යුතුය.

Contents of Proceedings : From 9.30 a.m. to 5.20 p.m. on 19.06.2008 Final set of manuscripts Received from Parliament : 4.00 p.m. on 27.06.2008 Printed copies dispatched : 01.07.2008 Morning

சந்தா ; ஹன்சாட் அதிகார அறிக்ைகயின் வᾞடாந்த சந்தா ᾟபா 2,178. ஹன்சாட் தனிப்பிரதி ᾟபா 18.15. தபாற் ெசலᾫ ᾟபா 2.50. வᾞடாந்த சந்தா ᾙற்பணமாக அத்தியட்சகர், அரசாங்க ெவளியீட்டᾤவலகம், இல. 132, மாயா அெவனிᾜ, கிᾞளப்பைன, ெகாᾨம்ᾗ 5 என்ற விலாசத்திற்கு அᾔப்பி பிரதிகைளப் ெபற்ᾠக்ெகாள்ளலாம். ஒவ்ேவாராண்ᾌம் நவம்பர் 30 ஆந் ேததிக்கு ᾙன் சந்தாப் பணம் அᾔப்பப்பட ேவண்ᾌம். பிந்திக் கிைடக்கும் சந்தா விண்ணப்பங்கள் ஏற்ᾠக்ெகாள்ளப்படமாட்டா.

දායක මුදල්: පාර්ලිෙම්න්තු විවාද වාර්තාවල වාර්ෂික දායක මිල රු.2178කි. පිටපතක් ෙගන්වා ගැනීම අවශɕ නම් ගාස්තුව රු. 18.15කි. තැපැල් ගාස්තුව රු. 2.50කි. ෙකොළඹ 5, කිරුළපන, මායා මාවත. අංක 132 රජෙය් පකාශන කාර්යාංශෙය් අධිකාරී ෙවත සෑම වර්ෂයකම ෙනොවැම්බර් 30දා ට පථම දායක මුදල් ෙගවා ඉදිරි වර්ෂෙය් දායකත්වය ලබාෙගන විවාද වාර්තා ලබාගත හැකිය. නියමිත දිෙනන් පසුව එවනු ලබන දායක ඉල්ලුම්පත් භාරගනු ෙනොලැෙබ්.

Subscription : The annual subscription for Official Report of Hansard is Rs. 2,178. A single copy of Hansard is available for Rs. 18.15. (Postage Rs. 2.50) Copies can be obtained by remitting in advance an annual subscription fee to the SUPERINTENDENT, GOVERNMENT PUBLICATION BUREAU, No. 132, Maya Avenue, Kirulapone, Colombo 5. The fee should reach him on or before November 30 each year . Late application for subscriptions will not be accepted.

ශී ලංකා රජෙය් මුදණ ෙදපාර්තෙම්න්තුෙව් මුදණය කරන ලදී.
